# <a name="quality-of-experience-review-guide"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-103">体验质量检查指南</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-103">Quality of Experience Review Guide</span></span>

<!-- Note that this link to the Word doc is intentionally NOT the aka.ms/qerquide link -->
<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-104">本指南是有关 Microsoft 团队和业务 online Skype 的驱动器值阶段。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-104">This guide is about the Drive Value phase for Microsoft Teams and Skype for Business Online.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-105">您可以本指南[下载的 Word 版本](https://github.com/MicrosoftDocs/OfficeDocs-SkypeForBusiness/blob/live/Teams/downloads/quality-of-experience-review-guide.docx?raw=true)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-105">You can [download a Word version](https://github.com/MicrosoftDocs/OfficeDocs-SkypeForBusiness/blob/live/Teams/downloads/quality-of-experience-review-guide.docx?raw=true) of this guide.</span></span>

## <a name="introduction"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-106">简介</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-106">Introduction</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-107">若要对在改善用户体验的影响大，组织需要实施的关键区域，如下图所示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-107">To have the greatest impact on improving the user experience, organizations need to operationalize the key areas that are shown in the following figure.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-108">其他领域包括标识操作任务、 建立质量指标的目标、 有助于确定要用于评估组织成功指标和根据需要将缩小调查的区域。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-108">Additional areas include identifying operational tasks, establishing targets for quality metrics, ascertaining the metrics to use to gauge organizational success, and narrowing areas of investigation as needed.</span></span>


<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-109">![键区域的用户体验质量包括音频、 可靠性、 用户调查、 设备和客户端。](media/qerguide-image-keyareas.png "键区域的用户体验质量包括音频、 可靠性、 用户调查、 设备和客户端。")</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-109">![Key areas for the quality of user experience include audio, reliability, user surveys, devices, and clients.](media/qerguide-image-keyareas.png "Key areas for the quality of user experience include audio, reliability, user surveys, devices, and clients.")</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-110">_图 1-本指南中介绍的密钥操作区域_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-110">_Figure 1 - Key operational areas covered throughout this guide_</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-111">通过不断地评估和补救此指南中所述的区域，您可以减少他们可能会产生负面影响的用户体验质量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-111">By continually assessing and remediating the areas described in this guide, you can reduce their potential to negatively affect the quality of your users’ experience.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-112">在部署中遇到的大多数用户体验问题可以分为以下类别：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-112">Most user-experience problems encountered in a deployment can be grouped into the following categories:</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-113">防火墙或代理配置不完整</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-113">Incomplete firewall or proxy configuration</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-114">Wi-Fi 覆盖范围较小</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-114">Poor Wi-Fi coverage</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-115">带宽不足</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-115">Insufficient bandwidth</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-116">VPN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-116">VPN</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-117">不一致或过期的客户端版本和驱动程序</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-117">Inconsistent or outdated client versions and drivers</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-118">未优化或内置的音频设备</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-118">Unoptimized or built-in audio devices</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-119">子网或网络设备存在问题</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-119">Problematic subnets or network devices</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-120">通过适当的规划和设计业务 online 部署团队或 Skype 之前，您可以减少的需要保持高质量体验的工作量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-120">Through proper planning and design before deploying Teams or Skype for Business Online, you can reduce the amount of effort that will be required to maintain high-quality experiences.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-121">本指南重点介绍使用作为主要工具，呼叫质量仪表板 (CQD) 联机报告和调查每个区域，以最大限度地应用和影响的音频特殊重点。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-121">This guide focuses on using the Call Quality Dashboard (CQD) Online as the primary tool to report and investigate each area, with a special emphasis on audio to maximize adoption and impact.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-122">对网络以提高音频体验任何改进还直接将翻译视频和桌面共享的改进。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-122">Any improvements made to the network to improve the audio experience will also directly translate to improvements in video and desktop sharing.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-123">若要加快您评估，提供[两个 curated 的 CQD 模板](https://aka.ms/qertemplates)： 一个用于管理所有网络，其他被过滤为仅托管 （内部） 网络。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-123">To accelerate your assessment, [two curated CQD templates](https://aka.ms/qertemplates) are provided: one is for managing all networks and the other is filtered for managed (internal) networks only.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-124">虽然所有网络模板报告配置为显示构建和网络信息，但它们仍可时您收集和上载构建信息的工作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-124">Although the All Networks template reports are configured to display building and network information, they can still be used while you work toward collecting and uploading building information.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-125">上载构建到 CQD 信息使服务能够增强报告通过添加自定义构建、 网络和位置信息时发送者内部从外部子网。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-125">Uploading building information into CQD enables the service to enhance reporting by adding custom building, network, and location information while differentiating internal from external subnets.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-126">有关详细信息，请参阅本指南后面的[构建映射](#building-mapping)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-126">For more information, see [Building mapping](#building-mapping) later in this guide.</span></span>

### <a name="intended-audience"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-127">目标访问群体</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-127">Intended audience</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-128">本指南旨在供合作伙伴和客户的利益干系人与角色如协作首席架构师、 顾问、 更改管理/采用专家、 支持/帮助台导致、 网络导致、 桌面潜在顾客和 IT 管理员。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-128">This guide is intended to be used by partner and customer stakeholders with roles such as Collaboration Lead/Architect, Consultant, Change Management/Adoption Specialist, Support/Help Desk Lead, Network Lead, Desktop Lead, and IT Admin.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-129">本指南旨在还使用指定的质量 champion(s)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-129">This guide is also intended to be used by the designated quality champion(s).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-130">有关详细信息，请参阅[质量冠军角色](4-envision-plan-my-service-management.md#the-quality-champion-role)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-130">For more information, see [the Quality Champion role](4-envision-plan-my-service-management.md#the-quality-champion-role).</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-133">**Office 365 全局管理员角色**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-133">**Office 365 Global Administrator role**</span></span> 

-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-134">**Skype 业务管理员角色**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-134">**Skype for Business Administrator role**</span></span> 

-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-135">**团队服务管理员角色**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-135">**Teams Service Administrator role**</span></span> 

-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-136">**团队 Communications 支持工程师角色**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-136">**Teams Communications Support Engineer role**</span></span> 

-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-137">**团队 Communications 支持专家角色**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-137">**Teams Communications Support Specialist role**</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-138">此外，您可以向 Office 365 用户帐户以允许访问报告功能仅分配下列角色。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-138">Alternatively, you can assign the following role to an Office 365 user account to allow access to reporting features only.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-139">**报告读取器：** 可以在 Office 365 管理中心，任何[Microsoft 365 采用内容包](https://support.office.com/article/Office-365-Adoption-content-pack-77ff780d-ab19-4553-adea-09cb65ad0f1f)中的报告和 CQD 报告中查看[活动报告](https://support.office.com/article/activity-reports-0d6dfb17-8582-4172-a9a9-aed798150263)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-139">**Reports Reader:** Can view all the [activity reports](https://support.office.com/article/activity-reports-0d6dfb17-8582-4172-a9a9-aed798150263) in the Office 365 admin center, any reports from the [Microsoft 365 Adoption content pack](https://support.office.com/article/Office-365-Adoption-content-pack-77ff780d-ab19-4553-adea-09cb65ad0f1f), and CQD reports.</span></span>

## <a name="what-is-quality"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-140">什么是质量？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-140">What is quality?</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-141">在讨论团队和 Skype for Business 中的质量，务必定义要实现常见了解的术语。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-141">When discussing quality in Teams and Skype for Business, it’s important to define the term to achieve a common understanding.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-142">此处定义质量，是服务指标和用户体验的组合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-142">Quality, as defined here, is a combination of service metrics and user experience.</span></span>

<!-- Note: need to update graphic-->
<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-143">![服务指标差流比率、 可靠性、 终结点/设备和客户端版本组成。用户体验质量的服务的用户的认知组成。](media/qerguide-image-whatisquality.png "服务指标差流比率、 可靠性、 终结点/设备和客户端版本组成。用户体验质量的服务的用户的认知组成。")</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-143">![Service metrics are made up of poor stream ratio, reliability, endpoints/devices, and client versions. The user experience is made up of the user's perception of the quality of the service.](media/qerguide-image-whatisquality.png "Service metrics are made up of poor stream ratio, reliability, endpoints/devices, and client versions. The user experience is made up of the user's perception of the quality of the service.")</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-144">_图 2-质量是什么？_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-144">_Figure 2 - What is quality?_</span></span>

### <a name="service-metrics"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-145">服务指标</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-145">Service metrics</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-146">服务指标包含基于客户端的特定指标。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-146">Service metrics consist of specific client-based metrics.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-147">期间每个呼叫，客户端收集遥测呼叫的信息，并提交可通过 CQD 或[呼叫分析](https://techcommunity.microsoft.com/t5/Skype-for-Business-Blog/Introducing-Call-Analytics/ba-p/57309)更高版本访问每个呼叫的结尾处的报告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-147">During each call, the client collects telemetry information about the call and submits a report at the end of each call that can be later accessed through CQD or [Call Analytics](https://techcommunity.microsoft.com/t5/Skype-for-Business-Blog/Introducing-Call-Analytics/ba-p/57309).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-148">这些指标包括：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-148">These metrics include:</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-149">质量欠佳的流速率</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-149">Poor Stream Rate</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-150">安装失败率</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-150">Setup Failure Rate</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-151">Drop 故障率</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-151">Drop Failure Rate</span></span>


#### <a name="poor-stream-rate"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-152">质量欠佳的流速率</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-152">Poor Stream Rate</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-153">不佳流率 (PSR) 表示组织的整体流具有质量不佳的百分比。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-153">The poor stream rate (PSR) represents the organization’s overall percentage of streams that have poor quality.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-154">此指标为了突出显示您的组织可以对努力向降低此值和改善用户体验，原因是最强大的影响精力处理的区域时查看 PSR[托管网络](#managed-vs-unmanaged-networks)是主要焦点。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-154">This metric is meant to highlight areas where your organization can concentrate effort to have the strongest impact toward reducing this value and improving the user experience, which is why [managed networks](#managed-vs-unmanaged-networks) are the primary focus when looking at PSR.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-155">外部用户是很重要，但调查不同组织的基础上。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-155">External users are important too, but investigation differs on an organizational basis.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-156">请考虑为外部用户提供最佳实践和调查独立于整个组织的外部呼叫。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-156">Consider providing best practices for external users, and investigate external calls independently from the overall organization.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-157">CQD 中的实际度量值随工作负荷，但出于的质量体验审阅我们重点主要关注的_音频质量欠佳的百分比_度量值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-157">The actual measurement in CQD varies by workload, but for the purposes of the Quality Experience Review we focus primarily on the _Audio Poor Percentage_ measurement.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-158">PSR 由五个下表中所述的网络指标平均值组成。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-158">PSR is made up of the five network metric averages described in the following table.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-159">对于分类为质量欠佳的流，只有一个指标需要超过定义的阈值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-159">For a stream to be classified as poor, only one metric needs to exceed the defined threshold.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-160">有关流分类过程的详细信息，请参阅[这篇文章](stream-classification-in-call-quality-dashboard.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-160">For more information about the stream classification process, see [this article](stream-classification-in-call-quality-dashboard.md).</span></span>

> [!Note]
> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-161">CQD 提供"质量欠佳由于..."</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-161">CQD provides the “Poor Due To…”</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-162">度量值，以便更好地了解哪些条件导致要归类为质量欠佳的流。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-162">measurements to better understand what condition caused the stream to be classified as poor.</span></span>


<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-163">_表 1 的音频质量较差的指标_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-163">_Table 1 - Audio poor quality metrics_</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-164">指标的平均值</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-164">Metric average</span></span>     | <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-165">说明</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-165">Description</span></span>     | <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-166">用户体验</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-166">User experience</span></span> |
|-------------|-----------------|-----------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-167">抖动\>30 ms</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-167">Jitter \>30 ms</span></span>        | <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-168">这是连续的数据包之间的延迟的平均更改。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-168">This is the average change in delay between successive packets.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-169">工作组和 for Business 的 Skype 可以适应通过缓冲抖动某些级别。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-169">Teams and Skype for Business can adapt to some levels of jitter through buffering.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-170">则只有当抖动超过缓冲参与者通知的抖动效果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-170">It’s only when the jitter exceeds the buffering that a participant notices the effects of jitter.</span></span>      | <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-171">到达不同的速度数据包会导致演讲者语音声自动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-171">The packets arriving at different speeds cause a speaker’s voice to sound robotic.</span></span>   |
| <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-172">数据包丢失率\>10%或 0.1</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-172">Packet loss rate \>10% or 0.1</span></span>        | <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-173">这通常被指的数据包丢失的百分比。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-173">This is often defined as a percentage of packets that are lost.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-174">数据包丢失直接影响音频质量 — 从小，个人丢失数据包背对背脉冲损失几乎没有任何影响的原因音频，完全去掉。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-174">Packet loss directly affects audio quality—from small, individual lost packets that have almost no impact to back-to-back burst losses that cause audio to cut out completely.</span></span>     | <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-175">在其预期目标被丢弃和未到达数据包会导致出现间隙媒体、 错过的音节和词中生成和断断续续视频和共享。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-175">The packets being dropped and not arriving at their intended destination cause gaps in the media, resulting in missed syllables and words, and choppy video and sharing.</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-176">往返时间\>500 ms</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-176">Round-trip time \>500 ms</span></span>        | <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-177">这是时间获取 IP 数据包从点 A，B 点和回点 a。此网络传播延迟限制到的物理距离的两个点之间的速度浅色，并包括执行的各种设备中的网络路径的额外开销。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-177">This is the time it takes to get an IP packet from point A to point B and back to point A. This network propagation delay is tied to the physical distance between the two points and the speed of light, and includes additional overhead taken by the various devices in the network path.</span></span>      | <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-178">时间过长到达其目标数据包会导致 walkie-talkie 效果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-178">The packets taking too long to arrive at their destination cause a walkie-talkie effect.</span></span>   |
| <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-179">NMOS 性能降低平均\>1.0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-179">NMOS degradation average \>1.0</span></span>         | <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-180">流的的平均[网络意味着平均意见得分 (NMOS)](https://docs.microsoft.com/previous-versions/office/communications-server/bb894481(v=office.12)#network-mos)性能降低。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-180">Average [Network Mean Opinion Score (NMOS)](https://docs.microsoft.com/previous-versions/office/communications-server/bb894481(v=office.12)#network-mos) degradation for the stream.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-181">代表影响收到导致 NMOS 要删除的多个点的音频的质量的网络丢失和抖动多少。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-181">Represents how much the network loss and jitter has affected the quality of received audio that caused the NMOS to drop by more than one point.</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-182">这是抖动数据包丢失的组合和 — 在较小者一定程度上 — 增加的往返时间。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-182">This is a combination of jitter, packet loss, and—to a lesser degree—increased round-trip time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-183">用户可能遇到以下症状的组合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-183">The user might be experiencing a combination of these symptoms.</span></span>   |
| <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-184">隐藏样本数的平均比率\>7%或 0.07</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-184">Average ratio of concealed samples \>7% or 0.07</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-185">使用生成的数据包丢失的总数的音频帧的样本隐藏样本数的音频帧的数目的平均比率。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-185">Average ratio of the number of audio frames with concealed samples generated by packet loss healing to the total number of audio frames.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-186">隐藏的音频示例是一种用于平滑通常将由丢弃的网络数据包突然转换技术。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-186">A concealed audio sample is a technique used to smooth out the abrupt transition that would usually be caused by dropped network packets.</span></span>      | <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-187">高值指示丢失隐蔽的重要级别已应用且导致音频失真或丢失。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-187">High values indicate that significant levels of loss concealment were applied and resulted in distorted or lost audio.</span></span>     |

#### <a name="setup-failure-rate"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-188">安装失败率</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-188">Setup Failure Rate</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-189">安装失败率，即所谓的_总呼叫安装失败百分比_度量值以 CQD，其中的媒体路径无法建立开头的呼叫的终结点之间的流数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-189">The setup failure rate, otherwise known as the _Total Call Setup Failure Percentage_ measurement in CQD, is the number of streams where the media path couldn’t be established between the endpoints at the start of the call.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-190">这表示无法建立任意媒体流。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-190">This represents any media stream that couldn’t be established.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-191">给定此处测量的用户体验的影响的严重性，旨在降低此值为零尽可能接近。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-191">Given the severity of the impact on the user experience measured here, the goal is to reduce this value to as close to zero as possible.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-192">此度量值高是在新部署中使用完整的防火墙规则更常见比成熟的部署，但仍，务必观看定期。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-192">A high value for this metric is more common in new deployments with incomplete firewall rules than a mature deployment, but it’s still important to watch on a regular basis.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-193">此指标的计算公式按照按提交成功的呼叫详细信息记录 (CDR) 的流总数未能设置划分流总数：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-193">This metric is calculated by taking the total number of streams that failed to set up divided by the total number of streams that submitted a successful call detail record (CDR):</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-194">**安装失败率**= 总呼叫失败的流计数的安装程序 / 总 CDR 可用 Stream 计数</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-194">**Setup Failure Rate** = Total Call Setup Failed Stream Count / Total CDR Available Stream Count</span></span>

#### <a name="drop-failure-rate"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-195">Drop 故障率</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-195">Drop Failure Rate</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-196">投递失败率，即所谓的_总呼叫而丢弃失败百分比_度量值以 CQD，是已成功建立流的媒体路径未正常终止的百分比。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-196">The drop failure rate, otherwise known as the _Total Call Dropped Failure Percentage_ measurement in CQD, is the percentage of successfully established streams where the media path didn’t terminate normally.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-197">这表示任何意外终止的媒体流。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-197">This represents any media stream that terminated unexpectedly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-198">虽然此方法的影响不作为流未能设置为严重，它会产生负面影响的用户体验。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-198">Although the impact of this isn’t as severe as a stream that failed to set up, it will negatively affect the user experience.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-199">突然和常见媒体下降而不是只可以有严重的影响的用户体验，它们会导致需要用户重新连接，从而导致丢失工作效率。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-199">Sudden and frequent media drops not only can have a severe impact on the user experience, they result in the need for users to reconnect, resulting in a loss in productivity.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-200">指标的计算公式按照总数除以成功设置流的总计的丢弃流：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-200">The metric is calculated by taking the total number of dropped streams divided by the total count of streams that set up successfully:</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-201">**Drop 失败率**= 总呼叫而丢弃流数 / 总呼叫安装成功流计数</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-201">**Drop Failure Rate** = Total Call Dropped Stream Count / Total Call Setup Succeeded Stream Count</span></span>

### <a name="define-your-target-metrics"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-202">定义您的目标指标</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-202">Define your target metrics</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-203">本节讨论一些我们使用评估如何服务遇到运行状况的核心服务指标。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-203">This section discusses some of the core service metrics that we use to assess how services experience health.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-204">通过不断地评估和驱动努力保留其定义目标下面这些指标，您将帮助确保您的用户体验一致、 可靠地呼叫质量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-204">By continually assessing and driving efforts to keep these metrics below their defined targets, you’ll help ensure that your users experience consistent, reliable call quality.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-205">为了帮助您入门，提供了以下目标。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-205">To get you started, the following targets are provided.</span></span>

</table>


<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-260">非常重要讨论和定义组织的目标，以满足业务目标。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-260">It's important to discuss and define your organization’s targets to meet your business objectives.</span></span>

### <a name="user-experience"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-261">用户体验</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-261">User experience</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-262">分析的用户体验比科学的多个图片，因为此处收集指标不始终意味着没有网络或服务的问题，但相反，它们只表明用户可以体验问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-262">Analyzing the user experience is more art than science, because the metrics gathered here don’t always mean that there’s a problem with the network or service but rather, they simply indicate that the user perceives a problem.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-263">Microsoft 提供的内置调查机制 — 已知作为速率我呼叫 (RMC) — 为了衡量整体用户体验。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-263">Microsoft offers a built-in survey mechanism—known as Rate My Call (RMC)—to help gauge overall user experience.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-264">RMC 将帮助您回答从用户的角度来看以下问题：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-264">RMC will help you answer the following questions from your users’ perspective:</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-265">是否知道如何使用解决方案？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-265">Do I know how to use the solution?</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-266">是解决方案易于使用且直观，并不支持我的日常通信需求？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-266">Is the solution easy to use and intuitive, and does it support my day-to-day communication needs?</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-267">解决方案帮助我完成工作？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-267">Does the solution help me get my job done?</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-268">我的解决方案的整体认知是什么？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-268">What’s my overall perception of the solution?</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-269">可以使用解决方案的任意位置的时间，无论我的位置？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-269">Can I use the solution at any point in time, regardless of where I am?</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-270">可设置和维护呼叫？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-270">Can I set up and maintain a call?</span></span>

#### <a name="rate-my-call"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-271">评价我的呼叫</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-271">Rate My Call</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-272">速率我呼叫 (RMC) 内置团队和 Skype for Business 和自动配置为向参与者显示一个在每个 10 呼叫或 10%之后。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-272">Rate My Call (RMC) is built into Teams and Skype for Business and is automatically configured to be displayed to the participant after one in every 10 calls, or 10 percent.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-273">此简短调查询问用户评价呼叫，并提供了为什么呼叫质量可能已不佳的很少的上下文。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-273">This brief survey asks the user to rate the call and provide a little context for why the call quality might have been poor.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-274">一个或两个评级被视为不佳、 三个到四个很好，并且五非常出色。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-274">A one or two rating is considered poor, three to four is good, and five is excellent.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-275">虽然有点滞后而指示器，这是错过服务指标可以的发现问题非常有用的指标。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-275">Although it’s somewhat of a lagging indicator, this is a useful metric for uncovering issues that service metrics can miss.</span></span>

> [!Note]
> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-276">直到教育用户可以通过通常提供良好的反馈，除了错误，响应对 RMC 调查响应回来为极其负值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-276">Until users are educated to respond to RMC surveys by giving good feedback in addition to bad, responses typically come back as overwhelmingly negative.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-277">大多数用户才响应时呼叫质量较差。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-277">Most users only respond when call quality is poor.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-278">因此，RMC 报告可能出现偏态不佳的一侧即使服务指标正常工作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-278">Because of this, your RMC reports might be skewed to the poor side even while service metrics are good.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-279">您可以使用 CQD RMC 用户响应报告和 CQD 模板中包括示例报告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-279">You can use CQD to report on RMC user responses, and sample reports are included in the CQD template.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-280">但是，他们不讨论在本指南的详细信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-280">However, they aren’t discussed in detail in this guide.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-281">有关 RMC Skype 业务 online 中的详细信息和用户培训，以提供有用 RMC 响应的指南，请参阅[本博客张贴内容](https://blogs.technet.microsoft.com/jenstr/2015/05/05/rate-my-call-in-skype-for-business-2015/)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-281">For more information about RMC in Skype for Business Online and guidance for educating users to give useful RMC responses, see [this blog post](https://blogs.technet.microsoft.com/jenstr/2015/05/05/rate-my-call-in-skype-for-business-2015/).</span></span>

#### <a name="client-and-device-readiness"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-282">客户端和设备的准备情况</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-282">Client and device readiness</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-283">您需要的实体的客户端和设备策略，以帮助确保您的用户具有一致和良好的用户体验。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-283">You need a solid client and device strategy to help ensure that your users have a consistent and positive user experience.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-284">几项主要原则驱动器每个准备策略。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-284">A few key principles drive each readiness strategy.</span></span>

##### <a name="client-readiness"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-285">客户端准备</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-285">Client readiness</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-286">强的客户端准备策略可确保您的用户，同时可享受最佳体验可能运行客户端的最新版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-286">A strong client readiness strategy ensures that your users are running the most recent version of the client while enjoying the best experience possible.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-287">Microsoft 定期修补程序业务客户端; Skype确保您保存它最新环境中对您的总体成功至关重要。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-287">Microsoft routinely patches the Skype for Business client; ensuring that you keep it up to date in your environment is vital to your overall success.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-288">也很重要记住到修补程序网络，视频、 USB 和音频驱动程序，因为它们经常正在被忽略，可能会影响用户的体验。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-288">It’s also important to remember to patch network, video, USB, and audio drivers, because they’re often overlooked and can affect the user’s experience.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-289">请考虑添加网络，Wi-fi，视频，USB，并为您当前的修补程序管理过程的音频驱动程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-289">Consider adding network, Wi-Fi, video, USB, and audio drivers to your current patch management process.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-290">我们建议您不让您落后按超过六个月的客户端版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-290">We recommend that you not let your client versions fall behind by more than six months.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-291">如果您使用的 Office 即单击，您正在已被保持最新的服务。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-291">If you’re using Office Click-to-Run, you’re already being kept up to date by the service.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-292">更高版本中本指南中，所述使用包含的[客户端版本](#client-versions)，以帮助您完成此过程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-292">Use the included [client versions](#client-versions), as described later in this guide, to assist you with this process.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-293">您还可以利用速率我呼叫示例报表，若要进一步增强您的客户端准备策略。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-293">You can also leverage the Rate My Call sample reports to further enhance your client readiness strategy.</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-294">目前，分发并自动更新通过 Azure 内容交付网络团队客户端和将保持最新的服务。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-294">Currently, Teams clients are distributed and updated automatically through the Azure Content Delivery Network and will be kept up to date by the service.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-295">由于此，客户端准备和调查活动不适用于团队。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-295">Due to this, client readiness and investigative activities aren’t applicable to Teams.</span></span>


##### <a name="device-readiness"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-296">设备就绪</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-296">Device readiness</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-297">任何一种单个策略会不影响您的设备准备策略以上的用户体验。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-297">No one single strategy can affect the user experience more than your device readiness strategy.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-298">大多数组织都高兴地从用户，删除不必要的设备 （例如，桌面电话或其他专用的音频设备），这通常是切换到团队或 Skype for Business 的核心业务理由。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-298">Most organizations are happy to remove unnecessary devices (for example, desk phones or other dedicated audio devices) from users, and this is often a core business justification for switching to Teams or Skype for Business.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-299">但是，这些相同的组织有时不愿意再提供替换设备，即使这些设备成本较低。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-299">However, those same organizations sometimes hesitate to provide replacement devices, even if those devices are less expensive.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-300">现代便携式计算机和 Pc，上述配有内置麦克风和扬声器，不进行了优化业务类语音 ip 电话 (VoIP)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-300">Modern-day laptops and PCs, though equipped with built-in microphone and speaker, aren’t optimized for business-class voice over IP (VoIP).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-301">这通常将创建不好的体验所有参与者，尤其是扬声器处于噪音环境。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-301">This often creates a poor experience for all participants, especially if the speaker is in a noisy environment.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-302">Microsoft 的设备认证计划可确保用户参与通过使用任何设备的团队或 for Business 的 Skype 认证的电话呼叫，它生成优于非认证的设备的体验。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-302">Microsoft’s device certification program ensures that when a user participates in a phone call by using any device certified for Teams or Skype for Business, it produces an experience that’s superior to a non-certified device.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-303">始终建议，团队和业务用户的 Skype 认证的耳麦或扬声器时使用参与桌面客户端通过语音呼叫。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-303">We always recommend that Teams and Skype for Business users use a certified headset or speaker when participating in a voice call through the desktop client.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-304">有关 Microsoft 认证设备的详细信息，查看有关[认证计划](/SkypeForBusiness/certification/overview)这些文章和查看[合作伙伴解决方案目录](https://partnersolutions.skypeforbusiness.com/solutionscatalog/personal-peripherals-pcs)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-304">For more information about Microsoft certified devices, review these articles about the [certification program](/SkypeForBusiness/certification/overview) and view the [partner solutions catalog](https://partnersolutions.skypeforbusiness.com/solutionscatalog/personal-peripherals-pcs).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-305">使用[设备报告](#devices)，此指南，以获取帮助管理您的设备的更高版本中所述。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-305">Use the [Devices report](#devices), described later in this guide, for assistance with managing your devices.</span></span>


### <a name="categories-of-quality"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-306">类别的质量</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-306">Categories of quality</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-307">留给高质量和可靠部署成功与否取决于您构建操作严格程度。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-307">The success of operationalizing a high-quality and reliable deployment depends on your building operational rigor.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-308">具体而言，特别注意图; 中所示的三个类别下面是本指南的焦点：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-308">Specifically, pay special attention to the three categories illustrated in the following figure; these are the focus of this guide:</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-309">**网络：** 音频质量重点差流比率 (PSR) 指标、 TCP 使用率、 有线和无线子网，并确定使用 HTTP 代理和 VPN。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-309">**Network:** Audio quality focused on the Poor Stream Ratio (PSR) metric, TCP usage, wired and wireless subnets, and identifying the use of HTTP proxies and VPN.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-310">**终结点：** 音频设备和客户端版本 (Skype for Business 仅)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-310">**Endpoints:** Audio devices and client versions (Skype for Business only).</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-311">**服务管理：** 此类别包括两个部分：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-311">**Service Management:** This category comprises two sections:</span></span>

    -   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-312">首先是 Microsoft 的责任管理和维护的团队和 Skype 的业务联机服务。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-312">First is Microsoft’s responsibility to manage and maintain the Teams and Skype for Business Online services.</span></span>

    -   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-313">第二个必须管理您的组织，以确保可靠地访问该服务，如更新构建信息和维护防火墙新的 Office 365 IP 地址，如基础结构添加到服务的任务。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-313">Second are tasks your organization must manage to ensure reliable access to the service, such as updating building information and maintaining firewalls for new Office 365 IP addresses as infrastructure is added to the service.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-314">![组织中的质量的类别： 服务管理、 终结点，以及网络。](media/qerguide-image-categories.png "组织中的质量的类别： 服务管理、 终结点，以及网络。")</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-314">![The categories of quality in an organization: service management, endpoints, and the network.](media/qerguide-image-categories.png "The categories of quality in an organization: service management, endpoints, and the network.")</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-315">_图 3-关键类别个团队和 Skype 业务 Online 部署_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-315">_Figure 3 - Critical categories for Teams and Skype for Business Online deployment_</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-316">下图概述每个类别必须执行的任务。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-316">The following graphic outlines the tasks you must execute for each category.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-317">我们建议您运行这些任务周一次，最少。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-317">We recommend that you run these tasks once a week, at a minimum.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-318">第一次执行这些任务需要比后续迭代的更多工作，因为这些类别的许多需要您验证您部署的配置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-318">The first time you perform these tasks will take more effort than subsequent iterations, because many of these categories require that you validate your deployment configurations.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-319">获得了所需的会议已定义的目标的状态后，执行这些任务将帮助您维护该状态。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-319">After you’ve achieved the state you want by meeting the targets you’ve defined, performing these tasks will help you maintain that state.</span></span>

<!--  This is a net new graphic, never was included in the online article. OOPS! -->
<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-320">![每个质量类别每周任务列表](media/qerguide-image-tasks.png "每个质量类别每周任务列表")</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-320">![List of weekly tasks per quality category](media/qerguide-image-tasks.png "List of weekly tasks per quality category")</span></span>

#### <a name="service-management-tasks"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-321">服务管理任务</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-321">Service management tasks</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-322">在云优先世界中，您必须执行某些服务管理任务，才能保持高品质用户体验。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-322">In a cloud-first world, you must perform certain service management tasks to maintain high-quality user experiences.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-323">确保没有足够带宽到达服务没有饱和 internet 链接，验证该服务质量 (QoS) 位于置于所有托管的网络区域，范围为这些任务和 — 最后 — 掌握[上的 Office 365 IP 范围防火墙](https://aka.ms/o365ips)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-323">These tasks range from ensuring there is sufficient bandwidth to reach the service without saturating internet links, validating that quality of service (QoS) is in place on all managed network areas, and—lastly—staying on top of [Office 365 IP ranges on firewalls](https://aka.ms/o365ips).</span></span>

#### <a name="network-tasks"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-324">网络任务</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-324">Network tasks</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-325">有两种类别的网络任务： 可靠性和质量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-325">There are two categories of network tasks: reliability and quality.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-326">可靠性着重于测量成功发起呼叫并保持联系的用户的能力。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-326">Reliability focuses on measuring the user’s ability to make calls successfully and stay connected.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-327">质量着重于发送到工作组和 Skype online 业务用户的客户端呼叫过程中和其结束后的聚合遥测数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-327">Quality focuses on the aggregated telemetry sent to Teams and Skype for Business Online by the user’s client during the call and after it has ended.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-328">给定关键影响可靠性具有的用户体验，请务必开始评估和深入质量之前调查这些指标。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-328">Given the critical impact that reliability has on the user experience, it’s important to begin assessing and investigating those metrics before diving into quality.</span></span> 

#### <a name="endpoints-tasks"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-329">终结点任务</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-329">Endpoints tasks</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-330">此类别中的主要任务验证上最近六个月，以确保用户获取对业务桌面客户端 Skype 连续优化的好处从桌面生成 for Business 的 Skype 运行哪些客户端版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-330">The main task in this category is validating which client versions are running Skype for Business on desktop builds from the last six months, to ensure users are getting the benefit of the continual optimizations made to the Skype for Business desktop client.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-331">此外，这可简化总体客户端管理任务，并提供一致的用户体验。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-331">Additionally, this simplifies overall client management tasks and provides a consistent user experience.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-332">其他重要区域是监控哪些设备普遍部署中，推动认证设备来提供最佳用户体验。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-332">The other important area is monitoring which devices are prevalent in your deployment and driving the use of certified devices to provide the best user experience.</span></span>


> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-333">目前，分发并自动更新通过 Azure 内容交付网络团队客户端和将保持最新的服务。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-333">Currently, Teams clients are distributed and updated automatically through the Azure Content Delivery Network and will be kept up to date by the service.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-334">客户端准备和调查活动不适用于团队。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-334">Client readiness and investigative activities aren’t applicable to Teams.</span></span>

## <a name="cqd-basics"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-335">CQD 基础知识</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-335">CQD basics</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-336">本节介绍使用 CQD 的基础知识。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-336">This section describes the fundamentals of working with CQD.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-337">指南授予的下列主题：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-337">Guidance is given for the following topics:</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-338">什么是 CQD？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-338">What is CQD?</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-339">使用 CQD 期望</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-339">Expectations using CQD</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-340">查找您的租户 ID</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-340">Finding your tenant ID</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-341">报告与 Skype 的 Microsoft 团队 for Business</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-341">Reporting on Microsoft Teams versus Skype for Business</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-342">首先与第二个分类</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-342">First versus second classifications</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-343">维度、 度量和筛选器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-343">Dimensions, measures, and filters</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-344">与呼叫流</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-344">Streams versus calls</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-345">良好的、 不佳的和未分类的呼叫</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-345">Good, poor, and unclassified calls</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-346">常见的子网</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-346">Common subnets</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-347">有关更深入的培训和资源，请参阅[附录](#other-resources)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-347">For more in-depth training and resources, see the [Appendix](#other-resources).</span></span>

### <a name="what-is-cqd"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-348">什么是 CQD？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-348">What is CQD?</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-349">呼叫质量仪表板 (CQD) 用于深入了解 Business services 使用团队和 Skype 进行的呼叫的质量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-349">You use the Call Quality Dashboard (CQD) to gain insight into the quality of calls made by using Teams and Skype for Business services.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-350">CQD 旨在帮助 Skype 的业务和团队 admins 和网络工程师优化网络，并将关闭关注质量、 可靠性和用户体验。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-350">CQD is designed to help Skype for Business and Teams admins and network engineers optimize the network and keep a close eye on quality, reliability, and the user experience.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-351">CQD 关注为整个组织的聚合遥测总体模式可以成为明显，允许员工做出明智的评估和规划修正活动以最大限度地影响。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-351">CQD looks at aggregate telemetry for an entire organization where overall patterns can become apparent, allowing staff to make informed assessments and plan remediation activities to maximize impact.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-352">CQD 提供报告提供深入总体质量、 可靠性和用户体验的指标。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-352">CQD provides reports of metrics that provide insight into overall quality, reliability, and user experience.</span></span>

> [!Note]
> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-353">CQD 不包含任何个人身份信息 (PII)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-353">CQD doesn’t contain any personally identifiable information (PII).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-354">PII 是可用自己或其他信息以确定、 联系人或找到某个人，或以识别个体在上下文中的信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-354">PII is information that can be used on its own or with other information to identify, contact, or locate a single person, or to identify an individual in context.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-355">本指南将帮助了解的核心概念的 CQD，以帮助最大限度地可以改进业务 online 与团队或 Skype 的用户体验的影响。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-355">This guide will help in understanding the core concepts of CQD to help maximize the impact you can make in improving your users’ experience with Teams or Skype for Business Online.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-356">[附录](#other-resources)中找不到其他 CQD 资源。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-356">Additional CQD resources can be found in the [Appendix](#other-resources).</span></span>

### <a name="expectations-using-cqd"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-357">使用 CQD 期望</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-357">Expectations using CQD</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-358">CQD，尽管可用于分析趋势和子网，不会始终提供了具体原因用于给定方案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-358">CQD, although useful for analyzing trends and subnets, doesn’t always provide a specific cause for a given scenario.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-359">若要了解这并使用 CQD 时设置正确期望至关重要：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-359">It’s important to understand this and set the correct expectation when using CQD:</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-360">CQD 不会为每个方案提供的根本原因。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-360">CQD won’t provide the root cause for every scenario.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-361">CQD 不包含电话系统或音频会议流。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-361">CQD won’t contain Phone System or Audio Conferencing streams.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-362">CQD 将指出以便进一步调查根据趋势。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-362">CQD will call out areas for further investigation based on trends.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-363">CQD 不包含任何 PII。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-363">CQD doesn’t contain any PII.</span></span>

### <a name="report-editions"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-364">报表版本</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-364">Report editions</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-365">有 CQD Online 中的两个报表版本： 摘要和详细。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-365">There are two report editions in CQD Online: Summary and Detailed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-366">使用位于屏幕顶部的蓝色栏中的下拉列表菜单打开报表 edition。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-366">Use the drop-down menu located in the blue bar at the top of the screen to open a report edition.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-367">在屏幕顶部显示选定的报表 edition 的名称。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-367">The name of the selected report edition is displayed at the top of the screen.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-368">摘要报告是静态的且不可编辑，下载，或导出。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-368">Summary reports are static and can’t be edited, downloaded, or exported.</span></span> 
-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-369">详细的报告可完全自定义，可以下载到导出或克隆的 CSV 文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-369">Detailed reports are fully customizable and can be downloaded to a CSV file, exported, or cloned.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-370">有关两种版本之间的差异的完整说明，请参阅[这篇文章](turning-on-and-using-call-quality-dashboard.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-370">For a full description of the difference between the two editions, see [this article](turning-on-and-using-call-quality-dashboard.md).</span></span>

![使用选择的摘要报告的下拉菜单](media/qerguide-image-reportcategories.png)

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-372">_图 4-CQD 报表类别_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-372">_Figure 4 - CQD report categories_</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-373">摘要报告分为四个类别：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-373">The summary reports are divided into four categories:</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-374">**摘要报告**分析质量趋势每天、 每月，与表格报告，以帮助标识具有质量不佳的子网的关注。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-374">**Summary Reports** focus on analyzing quality trends with daily, monthly, and table reports to assist with identifying subnets that have poor quality.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-375">当您首次登录到 CQD Online 时，这是默认登陆页面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-375">This is the default landing page when you first sign in to CQD Online.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-376">**Location-Enhanced 报告**分析质量趋势基于位置信息的关注。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-376">**Location-Enhanced Reports** focus on analyzing quality trends based on location information.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-377">若要使用这些报告，您必须已上载的生成文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-377">To use these reports, you must have uploaded a building file.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-378">**可靠性报告**分析可靠性趋势的音频、 视频、 基于视频的屏幕共享 (VBSS) 和应用程序共享的关注。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-378">**Reliability Reports** focus on analyzing reliability trends for audio, video, video-based screen sharing (VBSS), and app sharing.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-379">**用户体验质量报告**是详细 QER 模板的"简化向下"版本重点关注分析音频质量和可靠性的关键区域。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-379">**Quality of Experience Reports** are a “slimmed-down” version of the detailed QER templates, focusing on key areas for analyzing audio quality and reliability.</span></span>

### <a name="report-types"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-380">报告类型</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-380">Report types</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-381">您可以从两种类型的报告中 CQD，具体取决于您想要查看您的数据的方式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-381">You can choose from two types of reports in CQD, depending on how you want to view your data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-382">尽管本指南不涉及创建通过另一种类型的报表的具体情况，QER CQD 模板提供了供您使用的自定义图表和表报告的组合：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-382">Although this guide doesn’t cover the specifics of creating one type of report over another, the QER CQD templates provide a mix of customizable chart and table reports for you to use:</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-383">图表报表创建图形表示数据可视化格式的条形图。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-383">Chart reports create graphical bar charts to represent data in a visual format.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-384">图表报告最佳用于在给定的时间段内可视化数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-384">Chart reports are best used to visualize data over a given time period.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-385">表格报告可用于查看单个度量值和维度时将报告导出到 Microsoft Excel 中的操作的 CSV 文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-385">Table reports are useful for looking at individual measurements and dimensions when you export the reports to CSV files for manipulation in Microsoft Excel.</span></span>

### <a name="tenant-id"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-386">租户 ID</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-386">Tenant ID</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-387">某些 CQD 报告需要您的租户 id 包含筛选器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-387">Some CQD reports require that you include a filter for your tenant ID.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-388">由于 CQD 聚合数据的方式，联盟参与者遥测是包含。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-388">Due to the way CQD aggregates data, federated participant telemetry is included.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-389">尽管时分析趋势，这是非常重要，客户端和设备报告需要您筛选到特定租户排除联盟参与者的遥测数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-389">Although this can prove valuable when analyzing trends, client and device reports require that you filter data to a specific tenant to exclude federated participant telemetry.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-390">如果您不知道您的租户 ID，您可以使用下列方法之一找到它。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-390">If you don’t know your tenant ID, you can use one of the following methods to find it.</span></span>

> [!Note]
> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-391">这些方法都需要以下权限：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-391">These methods require the following permissions:</span></span><ul><li><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-392">全局管理员角色</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-392">Global Administrator Role</span></span></li><li><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-393">Skype 业务管理员角色</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-393">Skype for Business Administrator Role</span></span></li></ul>

#### <a name="azure-portal"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-394">Azure 门户</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-394">Azure portal</span></span>

1.  <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-395">登录到 Microsoft Azure 门户：<https://portal.azure.com></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-395">Sign in to the Microsoft Azure portal: <https://portal.azure.com></span></span>

2.  <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-396">选择**Azure Active Directory**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-396">Select **Azure Active Directory**.</span></span>

3.  <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-397">在**管理**下选择**属性**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-397">Under **Manage**, select **Properties**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-398">在**目录 ID**框中显示的租户 ID。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-398">The tenant ID is shown in the **Directory ID** box.</span></span>

#### <a name="azure-powershell"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-399">Azure PowerShell</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-399">Azure PowerShell</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-400">[安装 Microsoft Azure PowerShell 服务管理模块](https://docs.microsoft.com/powershell/azure/servicemanagement/install-azure-ps?view=azuresmps-4.0.0)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-400">[Install the Microsoft Azure PowerShell Service Management module](https://docs.microsoft.com/powershell/azure/servicemanagement/install-azure-ps?view=azuresmps-4.0.0).</span></span>

2. <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-401">打开 Azure PowerShell 命令窗口并运行以下脚本中，输入您的 Office 365 凭据出现提示时：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-401">Open an Azure PowerShell command window and run the following script, entering your Office 365 credentials when prompted:</span></span> 

   ```
   Login-AzureRmAccount
   ```

3. <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-402">在输出中列出的租户 ID。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-402">The tenant ID is listed in the output.</span></span>

#### <a name="skype-for-business-online-admin-center"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-403">Skype 的业务 Online 管理中心</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-403">Skype for Business Online Admin Center</span></span>

1.  <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-404">转到<https://portal.office.com>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-404">Go to <https://portal.office.com>.</span></span>

2.  <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-405">使用您的租户管理员组织帐户登录。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-405">Sign in with your tenant administrator organizational account.</span></span>

3.  <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-406">选择在**管理中心**下的**Skype for Business** 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-406">Select **Skype for Business** under **Admin Centers**.</span></span>

4.  <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-407">在欢迎页上的租户 ID 被列为**组织 ID** 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-407">The tenant ID is listed as **Organization ID** on the Welcome page.</span></span>

#### <a name="skype-for-business-online-using-powershell"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-408">Skype 业务 online 使用 PowerShell</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-408">Skype for Business Online using PowerShell</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-409">[设置 Windows PowerShell 的计算机](/SkypeForBusiness/set-up-your-computer-for-windows-powershell/set-up-your-computer-for-windows-powershell)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-409">[Set up your computer for Windows PowerShell](/SkypeForBusiness/set-up-your-computer-for-windows-powershell/set-up-your-computer-for-windows-powershell).</span></span>

2. <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-410">运行以下命令：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-410">Run the following command:</span></span>

   ```
   (Get-cstenant).tenantid
   ```

3. <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-411">租户 ID 显示为 GUID。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-411">The tenant ID is displayed as a GUID.</span></span>

### <a name="teams-vs-skype-for-business"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-412">团队与 Skype for Business</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-412">Teams vs. Skype for Business</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-413">CQD 可以报告团队和 Skype 的业务遥测。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-413">CQD can report on both Teams and Skype for Business telemetry.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-414">但是，可能会出现时要进行开发报表可以这样看待团队遥测分开 for Business 的 Skype 的次数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-414">However, there might be times when you want to develop a report to look at Teams telemetry separate from Skype for Business.</span></span>

#### <a name="summary-reports"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-415">摘要报告</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-415">Summary reports</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-416">若要修改摘要报告页上，可以这样看待仅团队或 for Business 的 Skype，顶部的屏幕上，选择**产品筛选器**下拉列表菜单，然后选择所需的产品。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-416">To modify the summary reports page to look at only Teams or Skype for Business, select the **Product Filter** drop-down menu from the top of the screen, and then select the product you want.</span></span>

![下拉菜单中显示筛选 CQD 报告按工作负载的选项](media/qerguide-image-productfilter.png)

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-418">_图 5-选择产品筛选器_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-418">_Figure 5 - Select a Product Filter_</span></span>

#### <a name="detailed-reports"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-419">详细的报告</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-419">Detailed reports</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-420">若要筛选所有的详细的报告，在浏览器栏中，该 URL 的末尾附加以下：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-420">To filter all detailed reports, in the browser bar, append the following to the end of the URL:</span></span>

```
/filter/[AllStreams].[Is Teams]|[FALSE]
```

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-421">**示例：**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-421">**Example:**</span></span>

```https://cqd.lync.com/cqd/#/1234567/2018-5/filter/[AllStreams].[Is Teams]|[FALSE]```

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-422">有关 URL 筛选器的详细信息，请参阅本节后面的[筛选报告](#filtering-reports)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-422">For more information about URL filters, see [Filtering reports](#filtering-reports) later in this section.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-423">若要筛选的单个详细的报告，添加筛选器``Is Teams``到报表，并将设置为 True 或 False。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-423">To filter an individual detailed report, add the filter ``Is Teams`` to the report and set it to True or False.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-424">有关详细信息，请参阅本节后面的[编辑报告](#editing-reports)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-424">For more information, see [Editing reports](#editing-reports) later in this section.</span></span>
