### <a name="managed-vs-unmanaged-networks"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-427">管理与非托管网络</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-427">Managed vs. unmanaged networks</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-428">默认情况下分类为外部 CQD 中的所有终结点。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-428">By default, all endpoints in CQD are classified as external.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-429">只要引入构建文件，我们可以开始查看托管终结点数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-429">As soon as a building file is introduced, we can begin to look at managed endpoint data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-430">如上文所述，CQD 中的网络定义为：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-430">As previously discussed, networks in CQD are defined as:</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-431">_托管网络_，通常称为内部或内，可以将影响和由组织控制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-431">A _managed network_, often referred to as internal or inside, can be influenced and controlled by the organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-432">这包括内部 LAN、 远程 WAN 和 VPN。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-432">This includes the internal LAN, the remote WAN, and VPN.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-433">_非托管的网络_，通常为外部或外部引用，无法影响或由组织控制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-433">An _unmanaged network_, often referred to as external or outside, can’t be influenced or controlled by the organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-434">非托管网络的示例是一个旅馆或机场网络。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-434">An example of an unmanaged network is a hotel or airport network.</span></span>

### <a name="dimensions-measures-and-filters"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-435">维度、 度量和筛选器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-435">Dimensions, measures, and filters</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-436">良好的 CQD 查询包含所有这三个以下参数：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-436">A well-formed CQD query contains all three of the following parameters:</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-437">**维度：** 我希望如何对数据透视。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-437">**Dimension:** How I want to pivot on the data.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-438">**度量值：** 我希望报告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-438">**Measure:** What I want to report on.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-439">**Filter:** 我希望如何降低查询的数据集返回。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-439">**Filter:** How I want to reduce the dataset the query returns.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-440">另一种方法可以这样看待这是_维度_是分组函数、_度量_是我感兴趣的数据，_筛选器_是我希望来缩小那些与我的查询相关的结果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-440">Another way to look at this is that a _dimension_ is the grouping function, a _measure_ is the data I’m interested in, and a _filter_ is how I want to narrow down the results to those that are relevant to my query.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-441">格式正确的示例是查询的**我的状态显示不佳流 [度量值] 的子网 [维度] 构建 6 [筛选器]**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-441">An example of a well-formed query is **Show me Poor Streams [Measure] by Subnet [Dimension] for Building 6 [Filter]**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-442">有关详细信息，请参阅[维度和度量 CQD 中可用](https://aka.ms/cqd-dm)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-442">For more information, see [Dimensions and measures available in CQD](https://aka.ms/cqd-dm).</span></span>

### <a name="first-vs-second"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-443">首先与秒</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-443">First vs. second</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-444">维度和度量 CQD 中的许多分类为第一个或第二个。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-444">Many of the dimensions and measures in CQD are classified as first or second.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-445">CQD 不使用呼叫者/被叫方字段 — 这些已重命名_首先_和_第二个_由于存在且之间的呼叫者和被叫方的步骤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-445">CQD doesn’t use caller/callee fields—these have been renamed _first_ and _second_ because there are intervening steps between the caller and callee.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-446">下面的逻辑确定为第一个标记所涉及的终结点：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-446">The following logic determines which endpoint involved is labeled as first:</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-447">**第一个**将始终保持 （会议服务器、 中介服务器，等） 中的服务器终结点如果服务器所涉及的流或呼叫中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-447">**First** will always be a server endpoint (Conference Server, Mediation Server, and so on) if a server is involved in the stream or call.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-448">**第二个**将始终为客户端终结点除非是两个服务器终结点之间的流。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-448">**Second** will always be a client endpoint unless the stream is between two server endpoints.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-449">如果两个端点都相同的类型，其中的选择是第一个基于用户代理类别的内部排序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-449">If both endpoints are the same type, the choice of which is first is based on internal ordering of the user agent category.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-450">这样可以确保排序的一致性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-450">This ensures the ordering is consistent.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-451">有关在这两个相同时，确定第一个或第二个终结点的详细信息，请参阅[维度和度量 CQD 中可用](https://aka.ms/cqd-dm)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-451">For more information about determining the first or second endpoint when they’re both the same, see [Dimensions and measures available in CQD](https://aka.ms/cqd-dm).</span></span>

### <a name="stream-vs-call"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-452">与呼叫流</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-452">Stream vs. call</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-453">您需要了解呼叫和流正确选择的维度或度量需要查看在 CQD 之间的差异。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-453">You need to understand the difference between a call and a stream to properly choose which dimensions or measures you’ll be looking at in CQD.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-454">尽管 CQD 的主焦点位于流，但也是可用基于调用的度量值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-454">Although CQD’s primary focus is on streams, call-based measurements are also available.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-455">**流：** 只有两个终结点之间存在_流_。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-455">**Stream:** A _stream_ exists between only two endpoints.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-456">没有为每个方向，只有一个流和两个流所需的通信。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-456">There is only one stream for each direction, and two streams are required for communication.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-457">流可用于调查建筑物、 网络或子网。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-457">Streams are useful for investigating buildings, networks, or subnets.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-458">在某些情况下，呼叫和 stream 的度量值的名称 （例如，呼叫安装流或呼叫丢弃流） 中使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-458">In some cases, both call and stream are used in the measurement’s name (for example, Call Setup Stream or Call Dropped Stream).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-459">这些仍将归类为流。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-459">These are still classified as streams.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-460">**呼叫：**_呼叫_是从所有参与者的所有流的分组。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-460">**Call:** A _call_ is a grouping of all streams from all participants.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-461">呼叫组成 — 至少 — 两个流。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-461">A call consists of—at minimum—two streams.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-462">单个呼叫将具有至少两个终结点，每个都与一个流的最小值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-462">A single call will have at least two endpoints, each with a minimum of one stream.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-463">是否维度或度量值引用呼叫或流的其他指导信息，请参阅[维度和度量 CQD 中可用](https://aka.ms/cqd-dm)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-463">For additional guidance on whether the dimension or measure is referring to a call or a stream, see [Dimensions and measures available in CQD](https://aka.ms/cqd-dm)</span></span>

### <a name="good-poor-and-unclassified-calls"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-464">良好的、 不佳的和未分类的呼叫</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-464">Good, poor, and unclassified calls</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-465">呼叫被分类为良好、 不佳，或者未分类。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-465">A call is categorized either as good, poor, or unclassified.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-466">我们来看片刻讨论更多详细信息中的每个。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-466">Let’s take a moment to talk about each one in more detail.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-467">**好或质量欠佳：** 好或质量欠佳的呼叫包含的包含一组完整的服务指标，完整的 QoE 报告已为其生成和服务收到呼叫。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-467">**Good or poor:** A good or poor call consists of a call that contains a complete set of service metrics, for which a full QoE report was generated and received by the service.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-468">确定流好或质量欠佳是所述的[之前在本指南](#poor-stream-rate)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-468">Determining whether a stream is good or poor is described [earlier in this guide](#poor-stream-rate).</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-469">**未分类：** 未分类的流不包含一组完整的服务指标。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-469">**Unclassified:** An unclassified stream doesn’t contain a full set of service metrics.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-470">这些可短呼叫 — 通常不超过 60 秒 — 其中无法计算平均值和未生成 QoE 报告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-470">These can be short calls—usually less than 60 seconds—where averages couldn’t be computed and a QoE report wasn’t generated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-471">未分类的呼叫的最常见原因是，没有任何数据包利用率很少。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-471">The most common reason for calls to be unclassified is that there was little to no packet utilization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-472">此示例将为的参与者加入会议静音和从不讲话时。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-472">An example of this would be a participant who joins a meeting on mute and never speaks.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-473">参与者是接收，但不是能传输媒体。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-473">The participant is receiving, but not transmitting, media.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-474">没有要传输的媒体，不会有任何指标可供 CQD 用于分类终结点的出站媒体流。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-474">Without media being transmitted, there won’t be any metrics available for CQD to use to classify the endpoint’s outbound media stream.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-475">有关流分类过程的详细信息，请参阅[这篇文章](stream-classification-in-call-quality-dashboard.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-475">For more information about the stream classification process, see [this article](stream-classification-in-call-quality-dashboard.md).</span></span>

### <a name="common-subnets"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-476">常见的子网</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-476">Common subnets</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-477">常见的子网是特定酒店或、 家庭网络、 热点和相似区域使用的专用子网。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-477">Common subnets are specific private subnets that are used by hotels, home networks, hotspots, and similar areas.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-478">由于其广泛使用会审难以这些子网。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-478">These subnets are difficult to triage due to their widespread use.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-479">如果您的组织使用这些常见的子网，我们建议您将该网络移到另一个子网。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-479">If your organization uses one of these common subnets, we recommend that you move that network to another subnet.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-480">这将使 CQD 中的报告以便更轻松。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-480">This will make reporting easier in CQD.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-481">当另有说明，已配置报告中的所有网络模板来排除这些子网，以消除这些作为质量不佳的一个来源。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-481">When noted, reports in the All Networks template have been configured to exclude these subnets to eliminate them as a source of poor quality.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-482">常见的子网定义如下;其影响组织的不同而有所不同。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-482">Common subnets are defined below; their impact will vary by organization.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-483">10.0.0.0/24</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-483">10.0.0.0/24</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-484">192.168.0.0/24</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-484">192.168.0.0/24</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-485">192.168.1.0/24</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-485">192.168.1.0/24</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-486">192.168.2.0/24</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-486">192.168.2.0/24</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-487">172.20.10.0/24</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-487">172.20.10.0/24</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-488">192.168.43.0/24</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-488">192.168.43.0/24</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-489">当调查托管的网络使用常见的子网，您需要使用第二个身本地 IP dimension 到组子网。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-489">When investigating a managed network that uses a common subnet, you’ll need to use the Second Reflexive Local IP dimension to group subnets.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-490">此维度包含终结点的公共 IP 地址。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-490">This dimension contains the endpoint’s public IP address.</span></span>

## <a name="cqd-online"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-491">联机 CQD</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-491">CQD Online</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-492">本节介绍访问 CQD 基础的知识。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-492">This section describes the fundamentals of accessing CQD.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-493">指南授予的下列主题：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-493">Guidance is given for the following topics:</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-494">联机访问 CQD</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-494">Accessing CQD online</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-495">入门 CQD</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-495">Getting started with CQD</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-496">编辑 CQD 中的报告</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-496">Editing reports in CQD</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-497">筛选 CQD 中的报告</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-497">Filtering reports in CQD</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-498">导入 CQD 中的报告</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-498">Importing reports in CQD</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-499">有关更深入的培训和资源，请参阅[附录](#other-resources)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-499">For more in-depth training and resources, see the [Appendix](#other-resources).</span></span>

### <a name="access-cqd-online"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-500">联机访问 CQD</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-500">Access CQD Online</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-501">您可以访问 CQD 三种方式之一：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-501">You can access CQD one of three ways:</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-502">转到<https://cqd.lync.com>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-502">Go to <https://cqd.lync.com>.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-503">转到**Microsoft 团队管理中心**，并选择链接到 CQD，如下图所示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-503">Go to **Microsoft Teams admin center** and select the link to CQD, as shown in the following illustration.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-510">当您首次浏览到 CQD 时，您将看到摘要报告页。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-510">When you first browse to CQD, you’ll see the Summary Reports page.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-511">自定义的详细的报告了大部分本指南中所述的报告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-511">Most of the reports described in this guide are custom detailed reports.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-512">若要开始使用详细的报告，选择页上，顶部的**摘要报告**，然后选择**详细的报告**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-512">To get started using the detailed reports, select **Summary Reports** at the top of the page, and then choose **Detailed Reports**.</span></span>

### <a name="editing-reports"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-529">编辑报告</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-529">Editing reports</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-530">当在报表的操作菜单上选择**编辑**时，您将打开查询编辑器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-530">When you select **Edit** on the action menu of a report, you’ll open Query Editor.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-531">每个报告备份到 CQD 的查询。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-531">Each report is backed by a query to CQD.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-532">报告是其查询返回的数据的可视化形式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-532">A report is a visualization of the data returned by its query.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-533">查询编辑器以供编辑报表的显示选项除了这些查询为用户界面，如下图所示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-533">The Query Editor is a UI for editing these queries in addition to the display options for the report, as illustrated in the following figure.</span></span>

### <a name="filtering-reports"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-549">筛选报告</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-549">Filtering reports</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-550">提供的模板包括几种内置查询和报告筛选器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-550">The templates provided include several built-in queries and report filters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-551">以下各节介绍整个模板中使用的最常见的筛选器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-551">The following sections describe the most common filters used throughout the templates.</span></span>

#### <a name="url-filter"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-552">URL 筛选器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-552">URL filter</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-553">您可以使用 URL 筛选器筛选器每个报告的特定维度。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-553">You can use a URL filter to filter every report for a specific dimension.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-554">最常见的 URL 筛选器用于筛选报告中排除联盟参与者遥测，或团队或 Skype 重点业务 online。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-554">The most common URL filters are used to filter reports to exclude federated participant telemetry, or focus on Teams or Skype for Business Online.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-555">建议的时使用筛选器，您书签它们以方便您参考。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-555">We recommend that when using filters, you bookmark them for easy reference.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-556">正在补救托管的建筑或联盟的终结点其中可能影响您的报告的网络时，从 CQD 报告中排除联合的数据很有用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-556">Excluding federated data from CQD reports is useful when you’re remediating managed buildings or networks where federated endpoints might influence your reports.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-557">若要实现 URL 筛选器，在浏览器地址栏中，该 URL 的末尾附加以下：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-557">To implement a URL filter, in the browser address bar, append the following to the end of the URL:</span></span>

```
/filter/[AllStreams].[Second Tenant Id]\|[YOUR TENANT ID HERE]
```

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-558">示例：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-558">Example:</span></span>  

```https://cqd.lync.com/cqd/#/1234567/2018-08/filter/[AllStreams].[Second Tenant Id]|[TENANTID]```

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-559">若要团队或 for Business 的 Skype 筛选报告，该 URL 的末尾附加以下：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-559">To filter the reports for Teams or Skype for Business, append the following to the end of the URL:</span></span>

```
/filter/[AllStreams].[Is Teams]|[TRUE | FALSE]
```

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-560">示例：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-560">Example:</span></span>

```https://cqd.lync.com/cqd/#/1234567/2018-08/filter/[AllStreams].[Is Teams]|[TRUE]```


> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-561">上面的示例 URL 供直观表示形式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-561">The URL examples above are for visual representation only.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-562">请使用的默认 CQD 链接<https://cqd.lync.com>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-562">Please use the default CQD link of <https://cqd.lync.com>.</span></span>


#### <a name="query-filters"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-563">查询筛选器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-563">Query filters</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-564">通过使用 CQD 中的查询编辑器实现查询筛选器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-564">Query filters are implemented by using the Query Editor in CQD.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-565">这些筛选器用于减少由 CQD，因此最小化的报表的总体大小和查询时间返回的记录数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-565">These filters are used to reduce the number of records returned by CQD, thus minimizing the report’s overall size and query times.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-566">这是对于筛选出非托管网络特别有用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-566">This is especially useful for filtering out unmanaged networks.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-567">筛选器中使用下面表列出正则表达式 (RegEx)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-567">The filters listed in the following table use regular expressions (RegEx).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-568">_表 3-查询筛选器_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-568">_Table 3 - Query filters_</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-569">筛选器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-569">Filter</span></span>         | <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-570">说明</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-570">Description</span></span>          | <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-571">CQD 查询筛选器示例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-571">CQD query filter example</span></span>      |
|----------------|----------------------|-------------------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-572">无空值</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-572">No blank values</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-573">某些筛选器无需对空值进行筛选选项。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-573">Some filters don’t have the option to filter for blank values.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-574">若要手动筛选空值，请使用空表达式，并设置为等于或不等于，筛选器，具体取决于您的需求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-574">To filter blank values manually, use the blank expression and set the filter to Equals or Not Equals, depending on your needs.</span></span>      | <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-575">第二个建筑物名称\< \> \^ \\s\*\$</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-575">Second Building Name \<\> \^\\s\*\$</span></span>                       |
| <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-576">常见的子网中排除</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-576">Exclude common subnets</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-577">如果没有分隔托管从非托管网络有效构建文件，将报告中包含家庭网络。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-577">Without a valid building file to separate managed from unmanaged networks, home networks will be included in the reports.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-578">这些主页的子网是它的控件的范围之外，可以快速排除从报表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-578">These home subnets are outside the scope of IT’s control and can be quickly excluded from a report.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-579">常见子网，如本指南中, 定义为 10.0.0.0、 192.168.1.0 和 192.168.0.0。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-579">Common subnets, as defined in this guide, are 10.0.0.0, 192.168.1.0 and 192.168.0.0.</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-580">第二个子网\< \> 10.0.0.0 \| 192.168.0.0 \| 192.168.1.0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-580">Second Subnet \<\> 10.0.0.0 \| 192.168.0.0 \| 192.168.1.0</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-581">仅查看内</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-581">View inside only</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-582">用于筛选 （内部） 托管或非托管 （外部） 的报告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-582">Used to filter a report for managed (inside) or unmanaged (outside).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-583">托管的 CQD 模板已与这些筛选器预配置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-583">The managed CQD template is already preconfigured with these filters.</span></span>       | <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-584">第二内 Corp = 内</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-584">Second Inside Corp = Inside</span></span>        |

#### <a name="report-filters"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-585">报告筛选器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-585">Report filters</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-586">通过对呈现报表可以在查询编辑器，或直接向报表添加筛选器实现报告筛选器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-586">Report filters are implemented by adding a filter to the rendered report either in the Query Editor or directly to the report.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-587">在模板整个中使用以下报告筛选器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-587">The following report filters are used throughout the template.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-588">_表 4-报告筛选器_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-588">_Table 4 - Report filters_</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-589">筛选器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-589">Filter</span></span>     | <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-590">说明</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-590">Description</span></span>                            | <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-591">CQD 报告筛选器示例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-591">CQD report filter example</span></span>         |
|------------|----------------------------------------|-----------------------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-592">Month</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-592">Month</span></span>      | <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-593">从一年开始第一张、 然后月份。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-593">Start with the year first, then month.</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-594">2017 10</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-594">2017-10</span></span>                           |

## <a name="import-the-cqd-templates"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-604">导入 CQD 模板</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-604">Import the CQD templates</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-605">本指南包含[两个 curated 的 CQD 模板](https://aka.ms/qertemplates)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-605">This guide includes [two curated CQD templates](https://aka.ms/qertemplates).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-606">这些模板加快 CQD 的使用情况，并为您提供快速利用 CQD 的功能，使用户团队或 Skype 对业务体验的影响的机会。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-606">These templates accelerate your usage of CQD and provide you an opportunity to quickly leverage CQD’s capabilities to make an impact on your users’ Teams or Skype for Business experience.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-607">所有网络模板，上述优化用于生成数据文件，可以使用您的工作收集和上载到 CQD，构建信息下一步部分中所述。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-607">The All Networks template, though optimized to work with a building data file, can be used while you work toward collecting and uploading building information into CQD, as described in the next section.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-608">**若要导入模板 (。CQDX) 到 CQD 联机**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-608">**To import the templates (.CQDX) into CQD Online**</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-609">转到<https://cqd.lync.com>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-609">Go to <https://cqd.lync.com>.</span></span>

2. <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-610">使用 Office 365 管理凭据进行身份验证。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-610">Authenticate by using your Office 365 Administrative credentials.</span></span>

   > [!NOTE]
   > <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-611">您必须具有 Office 365 全局管理员，业务管理员或报告读者角色访问 CQD Skype。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-611">You must have the Office 365 Global Administrator, Skype for Business Administrator, or Report Readers role to access CQD.</span></span> 

3. <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-612">选择顶部的页上，**摘要报表**菜单，然后选择**详细的报告**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-612">Select the **Summary Reports** menu at the top of the page, and then choose **Detailed Reports**.</span></span>

4. <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-613">在摘要窗格中，选择**导入**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-613">On the summary pane, select **Import**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-614">转到保存位置 CQDX，选择 CQDX 模板，然后选择**打开**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-614">Go to the CQDX saved location, select the CQDX template, and then select **Open**.</span></span>

5. <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-615">将模板上载后，变为弹出式窗口将显示消息"报表导入成功。"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-615">After the template is uploaded, a pop-up window will display the message “Report import was successful.”</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-616">选择**确定。**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-616">Select **OK.**</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-617">![通知模板已成功导入](media/qerguide-image-importmessage.png "通知模板已成功导入")</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-617">![Notification that the template was successfully imported](media/qerguide-image-importmessage.png "Notification that the template was successfully imported")</span></span>

6. <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-618">第二个 CQD 模板重复步骤 4 和 5。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-618">Repeat steps 4 and 5 for the second CQD template.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-619">每个用户导入 CQD 模板。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-619">The CQD templates are imported per user.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-620">如果其他用户需要使用报告，它们必须登录，并将模板导入其 CQD 实例。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-620">If additional users need to use the report, they must sign in and import the templates into their CQD instance.</span></span> 


## <a name="building-mapping"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-621">构建映射</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-621">Building mapping</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-622">在工作组或业务 Online 部署的 Skype，所有客户端的外部。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-622">In a Teams or Skype for Business Online deployment, all clients are external.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-623">具有，默认情况下，所有客户端都外部 CQD Online 中为报告，无论是否在公司内部网络连接，客户端隐含。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-623">That has the implication that by default, all clients are reported as outside in CQD Online, regardless of whether the client was connected on an internal corporate network.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-624">当您处理 CQD，您需要知道终结点的位置和它已连接到网络可以管理或网络是否无法管理 — 您可以管理假设正在您只会提高网络。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-624">When you work with CQD, you need to know the location of an endpoint and whether it was connected to a network you can manage or a network you can’t manage—the assumption being that you can only improve networks you can manage.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-625">通过将子网和构建信息上载到 CQD Online，您启用 CQD 以确定是否终结点已连接到托管公司 / 内部网络或非托管外部/网络。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-625">By uploading subnet and building information to CQD Online, you enable CQD to determine whether the endpoint was connected to an internal corporate/managed network or to an external/unmanaged network.</span></span>

### <a name="building-data-file-structure"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-626">构建数据文件结构</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-626">Building data file structure</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-627">您上载的数据文件的格式必须满足以下要求才能通过在上载之前验证检查。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-627">The format of the data file you upload must meet the following requirements to pass the validation check before uploading.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-628">该文件必须 TSV 文件 — 这意味着，对于每一行，每个列分隔制表符 — 或每个列并用逗号分隔的 CSV 文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-628">The file must be either a TSV file—which means that for each row, each column is separated by a Tab character—or a CSV file in which each column is separated by a comma.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-629">文件不能超过 50 MB。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-629">The file can’t be larger than 50 MB.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-630">数据的内容文件*不能包括表格标题*。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-630">The content of the data file *must not include table headers*.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-631">换句话说，数据文件的第一行必须实际数据，不列标题，例如"网络"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-631">In other words, the first line of the data file must be real data, not column headings such as “Network.”</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-632">每个列的数据类型仅可以是字符串、 号码或 Bool。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-632">For each column, the data type can only be String, Number, or Bool.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-633">如果数据类型是数字，值必须是数值;如果是 Bool，值必须是 0 或 1。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-633">If the data type is Number, the value must be a numeric value; if it’s Bool, the value must be either 0 or 1.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-634">每个列的数据类型为 String，如果数据可以为空 (但仍必须用相应的分隔符分隔 — 即，制表符或逗号分隔)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-634">For each column, if the data type is String, the data can be empty (but still must be separated by an appropriate delimiter—that is, a Tab character or comma).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-635">这只是分配该字段空字符串值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-635">This just assigns that field an empty string value.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-636">必须为每个行的 14 列。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-636">There must be 14 columns for each row.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-637">每个列必须具有下表中所述的数据类型和列都必须包含在表中列出的顺序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-637">Each column must have the data type described in the following table, and the columns must be in the order listed in the table.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-638">_表 5-构建文件结构_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-638">_Table 5 - Building file structure_</span></span>

|--------------------|-----------|---------------------------|-------------|

| <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-691">InsideCorp</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-691">InsideCorp</span></span>         | <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-692">Bool</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-692">Bool</span></span>      | <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-693">1</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-693">1</span></span>                         | <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-694">必需</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-694">Required</span></span>    |
| <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-695">ExpressRoute</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-695">ExpressRoute</span></span>       | <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-696">Bool</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-696">Bool</span></span>      | <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-697">0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-697">0</span></span>                         | <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-698">必需</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-698">Required</span></span>    |

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-699">\*时不需要 CQD，模板配置为显示构建和网络名称。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-699">\*While not required by CQD, the templates are configured to display Building and Network name.</span></span>

#### <a name="supernetting"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-700">Supernetting</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-700">Supernetting</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-701">您可以使用 supernetting，通常称作无类别域际路由 (选择 CIDR，) 来代替定义每个子网。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-701">You can use supernetting, commonly called Classless Inter-Domain Routing (CIDR,) in place of defining each subnet.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-702">*Supernet*是共享单个路由前缀的几个子网的组合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-702">A *supernet* is a combination of several subnets that share a single routing prefix.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-703">而不是添加的每个子网的项，您可以使用 supernetted 地址。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-703">Instead of adding an entry for each subnet, you can use the supernetted address.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-704">支持 supernetting，但我们不建议使用它。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-704">Supernetting is supported, but we don’t recommend using it.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-705">例如，Contoso 市场营销构建组成下的子网：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-705">For example, Contoso’s marketing building is made up of the subnets below:</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-706">10.1.0.0/24—first floor</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-706">10.1.0.0/24—first floor</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-707">10.1.1.0/24—second floor</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-707">10.1.1.0/24—second floor</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-708">10.1.2.0/24—third floor</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-708">10.1.2.0/24—third floor</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-709">10.1.3.0/24—fourth floor</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-709">10.1.3.0/24—fourth floor</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-710">而不是添加的每个子网的项，您可以使用 supernetted 地址 — 在此示例中，10.1.0.0/22。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-710">Instead of adding an entry for each subnet, you can use the supernetted address—in this example, 10.1.0.0/22.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-711">网络 = 10.1.0.0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-711">Network = 10.1.0.0</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-712">网络范围 = 22</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-712">Network Range = 22</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-713">下面是实现 supernetting 之前应考虑的几个事项：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-713">Here are a few things to consider before you implement supernetting:</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-714">Supernetting 仅可在具有 8 位到 28 位掩码的子网映射。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-714">Supernetting can only be used in a subnet mapping with 8-bit to 28-bit mask.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-715">Supernetting 提前，需要较少的时间，但它代价减少您的数据的丰富功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-715">Supernetting takes less time up front, but it comes at the cost of reducing the richness of your data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-716">假设没有质量问题涉及子网 200.1.2.0。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-716">Let’s say there’s a quality problem involving subnet 200.1.2.0.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-717">如果您实现 supernetting，您不知道中构建子网的位置或 （例如，实验室） 是哪种类型的网络。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-717">If you implemented supernetting, you won’t know where in the building the subnet is located or what type of network it is (for example, a lab).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-718">如果您具有定义生成的所有子网，并上载 floor 位置信息，您可以看到的差异。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-718">If you’d defined all the subnets for a building and uploaded floor location information, you’d be able to see that distinction.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-719">请务必确保 supernetted 地址正确，且不捕获不需要的子网。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-719">It’s important to ensure that the supernetted address is correct and isn’t catching unwanted subnets.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-720">是非常常见在数据中查找 192.168.0.0。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-720">It’s quite common to find 192.168.0.0 in data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-721">对于许多组织，这表明该用户是在家。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-721">For many organizations, this indicates that the user is at home.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-722">对于其他人，这是分支办公地点的 IP 地址方案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-722">For others, this is the IP address scheme for a satellite office.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-723">如果您的组织具有使用此配置的办公室，不包含该生成文件中因为很难区分使用常见的子网家庭和内部网络。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-723">If your organization does have offices that use this configuration, don’t include it in your building file because it’s difficult to distinguish between home and internal networks by using common subnets.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-724">请参阅关于[常见子网](#common-subnets)，本指南前面的部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-724">See the section about [common subnets](#common-subnets), earlier in this guide.</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-725">网络范围可以用于表示 supernet。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-725">The network range can be used to represent a supernet.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-726">所有新生成数据文件上载将检查的任何重叠的区域。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-726">All new building data file uploads will be checked for any overlapping ranges.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-727">如果先前已上载的生成文件，您应下载当前文件和上载再次来确定任何重叠并修复问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-727">If you’ve previously uploaded a building file, you should download the current file and upload it again to identify any overlaps and fix the issue.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-728">重叠之前上载文件的任何情况可能会导致建筑物报告中的子网的错误映射。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-728">Any overlap in previously uploaded files might result in the wrong mappings of subnets to buildings in the reports.</span></span>

#### <a name="vpn"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-729">VPN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-729">VPN</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-730">体验质量 (QoE) 数据的客户端发送到 Office 365 — 即 CQD 数据源自 — 包含一个 VPN 标志。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-730">The quality of experience (QoE) data that clients send to Office 365—which is where CQD data is sourced from—includes a VPN flag.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-731">CQD 将看到此作为第一个 VPN 和第二个 VPN 维度。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-731">CQD will see this as the First VPN and Second VPN dimensions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-732">但是，此标志依赖于 VPN 供应商的 VPN 网络适配器注册为远程访问适配器到 Windows 报告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-732">However, this flag relies on VPN vendors’ reporting to Windows that the VPN network adapter registered is a Remote Access adapter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-733">并非所有 VPN 供应商正确都注册远程访问适配器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-733">Not all VPN vendors properly register Remote Access adapters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-734">因此，您可能无法使用内置的 VPN 查询筛选器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-734">Because of this, you might not be able to use the built-in VPN query filters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-735">有两种方法适应 VPN 中构建的子网信息文件：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-735">There are two approaches to accommodating VPN subnets in the building information file:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-736">在此字段中使用的文本"VPN"，为 VPN 子网定义**网络名称**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-736">Define a **Network Name** by using the text “VPN” in this field for VPN subnets.</span></span>

  ![定义如何创建 VPN 子网的 CQD 报告](media/qerguide-image-vpnnetworkname.png)

  <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-738">_图 12-VPN 使用网络名称_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-738">_Figure 12 - VPN using network name_</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-739">在此字段中使用的文本"VPN"，为 VPN 子网定义**建筑物名称**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-739">Define a **Building Name** by using the text “VPN” in this field for VPN subnets.</span></span>

  ![定义如何创建构建定义构成 VPN 子网的 CQD 报表。](media/qerguide-image-vpnbuildingname.png)

  <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-741">_图 13-使用建筑物名称的 VPN_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-741">_Figure 13 - VPN using building name_</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-742">某些 VPN 实现不准确报告子网信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-742">Certain VPN implementations don’t accurately report subnet information.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-743">如果在您的报告，我们建议时将 VPN 子网添加到该生成文件，而不是一个条目的子网，将发生这种情况作为单独的 32 位网络的 VPN 子网中添加单独对每个地址条目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-743">If this occurs in your reporting, we recommend that when you add a VPN subnet to the building file, instead of one entry for the subnet, add separate entries for each address in the VPN subnet as a separate 32-bit network.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-744">每行可以有相同的构建元数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-744">Each row can have the same building metadata.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-745">例如，而不是一个 172.16.18.0/24 行中，您必须 253 行，通过从 172.16.18.1/32 通过 172.16.18.254/32，包括每个地址的一行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-745">For example, instead of one row for 172.16.18.0/24, you have 253 rows, with one row for each address from 172.16.18.1/32 through 172.16.18.254/32, inclusive.</span></span>


> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-746">已知 VPN 连接错误识别的网络连接，如有线基础的 internet 连接时无线。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-746">VPN connections have been known to misidentify the network connection as wired when the underlying internet connection is wireless.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-747">当通过 VPN 连接看质量，您不能假定已准确地发现的连接类型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-747">When looking at quality over VPN connections, you can’t assume that the connection type has been accurately identified.</span></span>

### <a name="uploading-building-information"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-748">上载构建信息</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-748">Uploading building information</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-749">CQD 摘要报告仪表板中包括的在右上角 （查找齿轮图标） 中选择的**租户数据上载**link 标记访问**租户数据上载**页面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-749">The CQD Summary Reports dashboard includes a **Tenant Data Upload** page, accessed by selecting the **Tenant Data Upload** link tag in the upper-right corner (look for the gear icon).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-750">此页用于为 admins 上载他们自己的信息，如映射的 IP 地址和地理信息，映射的每个无线访问点和其 MAC 地址，等等。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-750">This page is used for admins to upload their own information, such as mapping of IP address and geographical information, mapping each wireless access point and its MAC address, and so on.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-751">转到 CQD 联机通过浏览到<https://cqd.lync.com>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-751">Go to CQD Online by browsing to <https://cqd.lync.com>.</span></span>

2. <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-752">在右上角，选择齿轮图标，然后从**摘要报告**页中选择**租户数据上载**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-752">Select the gear icon in the upper-right corner, and choose **Tenant Data Upload** from the **Summary Reports** page.</span></span>

   ![出现时正在上载数据对话框](media/qerguide-image-tenantdataupload.png)

   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-754">_图 14-租户数据上载菜单_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-754">_Figure 14 - Tenant Data Upload menu_</span></span>

3. <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-755">此外，如果这是首次访问 CQD，您将需要上载生成数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-755">Alternatively, if this is your first time visiting CQD, you’ll be asked to upload building data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-756">您可以**立即上载**迅速导航至**租户数据上载**页上选择。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-756">You can select **Upload Now** to quickly navigate to the **Tenant Data Upload** page.</span></span>

   ![通知用户上载生成数据的横幅](media/qerguide-image-buildingdatauploadbanner.png)

   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-758">_图 15-构建数据上载横幅_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-758">_Figure 15 - Building data upload banner_</span></span>

4. <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-759">在**租户数据上载**页上，选择**浏览**选择数据文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-759">On the **Tenant Data Upload** page, select **Browse** to choose a data file.</span></span>

5. <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-760">在选择数据文件之后, 指定**开始日期**和 （可选） 指定结束日期。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-760">After selecting a data file, specify **Start date** and, optionally, specify an end date.</span></span>

6. <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-761">选择后**开始日期**，选择**上载**以将文件上载到 CQD。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-761">After selecting **Start date**, select **Upload** to upload the file to CQD.</span></span> <br><br><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-762">上载文件之前，对其进行验证。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-762">Before the file is uploaded, it’s validated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-763">如果验证失败，请求您更正文件显示一条错误消息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-763">If validation fails, an error message is displayed requesting that you correct the file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-764">下图显示在数据文件中的列数不正确时出现错误。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-764">The following figure shows an error occurring when the number of columns in the data file is incorrect.</span></span>

   ![导入构建数据时显示一条错误消息对话框中的示例](media/qerguide-image-buildingdatauploaderror.png)
 
   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-766">_图 16-构建数据上载错误_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-766">_Figure 16 - Building data upload error_</span></span>

7. <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-767">如果验证过程中不发生任何错误，将会成功上载文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-767">If no errors occur during validation, the file upload will succeed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-768">您随后可以看到**我上载**表，其中显示所有上载文件的完整列表，该页面底部当前租户中上载的数据文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-768">You can then see the uploaded data file in the **My uploads** table, which shows the full list of all uploaded files for the current tenant at the bottom of that page.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-769">可能需要四个小时完成处理的生成文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-769">It can take up to four hours to finish processing the building file.</span></span> <br><br> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-770">如果您已上载的生成文件，而需要添加子网可能已丢失或排除，通过添加新的子网中修改的原始文件，删除当前文件，并重新上载新编辑过的文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-770">If you’ve already uploaded a building file and need to add subnets that might have been missed or excluded, modify the original file by adding the new subnets, remove the current file, and re-upload the newly edited file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-771">可以有一个活动生成 CQD 中的数据文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-771">There can be only one active building data file in CQD.</span></span> 


### <a name="updating-a-building-file"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-772">更新构建文件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-772">Updating a building file</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-773">添加新的子网和其构建信息作为其有空时收集构建和子网信息，管理员将通常上载构建文件中的多个迭代随着时间的推移。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-773">While gathering building and subnet information, administrators will often upload the building file in multiple iterations over time, adding new subnets and their building information as it becomes available.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-774">当发生这种情况时，您需要重新上载您构建的文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-774">When this occurs, you’ll need to re-upload your building file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-775">此过程就像在上一节，如下面一节中所述的少数例外中所述初始上载。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-775">This process is like the initial upload as described in the previous section, with a few exceptions as noted in the following section.</span></span>

> [!Important]
> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-776">一次，只有一个生成文件可处于活动状态。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-776">Only one building file can be active at a time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-777">多个构建文件不累积。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-777">Multiple building files aren’t cumulative.</span></span>

#### <a name="adding-net-new-subnets"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-778">添加新的网络子网</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-778">Adding net new subnets</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-779">有时您需要将新的网络子网添加到最初不属于您的网络拓扑的 CQD 的次数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-779">There are times when you’ll need to add net new subnets to CQD that weren’t originally part of your network topology.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-780">若要添加新的网络子网，请执行下列操作 CQD 租户数据上载门户中：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-780">To add net new subnets, do the following in the CQD Tenant Data Upload portal:</span></span>

1.  <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-781">编辑的原始的生成文件，并提供发生至少一天前新网络子网已获得的结束日期。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-781">Edit the original building file and provide an end date that occurs at least one day before the net new subnets were acquired.</span></span>
2.  <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-782">如果您没有最新副本，请下载的原始文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-782">Download the original file, if you don’t already have an up-to-date copy.</span></span>
3.  <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-783">将新的网络子网追加到原始的生成文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-783">Append the net new subnets to the original building file.</span></span>
4.  <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-784">按照与上述，相同的进程将修改新的生成文件上载，并将设置一天以前的生成文件结束后的开始日期。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-784">Upload the newly modified building file following the same process as above, and set the start date for one day after the previous building file ends.</span></span>

#### <a name="updating-the-current-building-file"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-785">更新当前的生成文件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-785">Updating the current building file</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-786">如果已上载的生成文件，但您需要添加缺少的子网，请执行下列操作 CQD 租户数据上载门户中：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-786">If a building file is already uploaded but you need to add missing subnets, do the following in the CQD Tenant Data Upload portal:</span></span>

1.  <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-787">如果您没有最新副本，请下载的原始文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-787">Download the original file, if you don’t already have an up-to-date copy.</span></span>
2.  <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-788">在 CQD 中删除当前的文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-788">Remove the current file in CQD.</span></span>
3.  <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-789">附加到原始文件的新的子网。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-789">Append the new subnets to the original file.</span></span>
4.  <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-790">上载生成文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-790">Upload the building file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-791">请务必设置的开始日期为至少八个月以前以便 CQD 将处理的历史数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-791">Be sure to set the start date to at least eight months prior so that CQD will process historical data.</span></span>

### <a name="missing-subnets"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-792">缺少的子网</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-792">Missing subnets</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-793">上载托管网络的构建信息后，每个托管的网络应具有构建关联。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-793">After you upload building information for managed networks, every managed network should have a building association.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-794">但是，这不会始终是大小写;通常情况下，会丢失一些子网。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-794">However, this won’t always be the case; typically, a few subnets are missed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-795">本节介绍如何验证这些缺少的网络。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-795">This section covers how to validate those missing networks.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-796">浏览到 CQD Online 中的**详细的报告**页面，并导航到 CQD 模板中包括**缺少子网报告**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-796">Browse to the **Detailed Reports** page in CQD Online and navigate to the **Missing Subnet Report** included in the CQD templates.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-797">此提供构建数据中未定义的 10 或更多音频流的所有子网文件和被标记为外部。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-797">This presents all the subnets with 10 or more audio streams that aren’t defined in the building data file and are being marked as outside.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-798">确保在此列表中没有托管的网络。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-798">Ensure that there are no managed networks in this list.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-799">如果子网丢失，更新原始构建数据文件并将其重新上载到 CQD。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-799">If subnets are missing, update the original building data file and re-upload it to CQD.</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-800">您需要将您的租户 ID 作为**第二个租户 ID**的查询筛选器添加到此报告可以筛选报表，以只查看您的组织的租户数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-800">You’ll need to add your tenant ID as a query filter for **Second Tenant ID** to this report to filter the report to view only your organization’s tenant data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-801">否则，报告将显示联合的子网。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-801">Otherwise, the report will show federated subnets.</span></span>

> [!NOTE] 
> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-802">一定要调整到本月的月年报告筛选器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-802">Be sure to adjust the Month Year report filter to the current month.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-803">选择**编辑**，然后调整**月年**报告筛选器，以保存新默认的月份。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-803">Select **Edit**, and adjust the **Month Year** report filter to save the new default month.</span></span>

![报告显示未包括在 CQD 构建数据文件的显示使用情况的子网。](media/qerguide-image-missingbuildingreport.png)

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-805">_图 17-丢失生成报表_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-805">_Figure 17 - Missing Building Report_</span></span>

### <a name="building-mapping-tools"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-806">构建映射工具</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-806">Building mapping tools</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-807">面对事实吧，很难出您的组织中的子网映射。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-807">Let’s face it, mapping out subnets in your organization can be difficult.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-808">大型全局网络非常复杂，与其他团队管理其各自的区域，也可能没有单一网络拓扑的真实性的源。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-808">Large global networks are very complex, with different teams managing their respective regions, and there might be no single source of truth for the network topology.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-809">有两个工具可用来帮助的起始构建映射练习，以下各节中所述。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-809">There are two tools available to assist with starting the building mapping exercise, described in the following sections.</span></span>

#### <a name="cqd-tools"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-810">CQD 工具</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-810">CQD tools</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-811">这些工具基于 PowerShell，可以利用 Active Directory (AD) 站点和服务和 Microsoft DHCP 服务来帮助预填充您构建的文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-811">These tools are based on PowerShell and can leverage Active Directory (AD) Sites and Services and Microsoft DHCP services to help pre-populate your building file.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-812">这些工具有助于执行以下任务：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-812">These tools will help with the following tasks:</span></span>

1.  <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-813">查询 AD 站点和服务，并构建基于创建文件中包含的信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-813">Query AD Sites and Services, and create a building file based on the information contained within.</span></span>
2.  <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-814">查询 Microsoft DHCP 服务器或服务器提取子网信息并自动创建的生成文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-814">Query a Microsoft DHCP server or servers to pull subnet information and automatically create a building file.</span></span>
3.  <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-815">验证现有的生成文件，检查复制和重叠。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-815">Validate an existing building file, checking for duplicates and overlaps.</span></span>
4.  <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-816">查找未映射的子网中 CQD。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-816">Find unmapped subnets in CQD.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-817">有关此工具的详细信息，请参阅[本博客张贴内容](https://aka.ms/cqdtools)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-817">For more information about this tool, see [this blog post](https://aka.ms/cqdtools).</span></span>

#### <a name="network-planner"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-818">Network Planner</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-818">Network Planner</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-819">网络计划工具确定和组织您的网络要求云语音部署只通过几次简单的步骤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-819">The Network Planner determines and organizes your network requirements for your Cloud Voice deployment in just a few simple steps.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-820">通过提供您的组织的网络的详细信息和云语音使用，可以获取计算的网络要求的近似云语音部署、 管理和导出的报告，这些详细信息和查看以便进一步调查及后续步骤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-820">By providing your organization's networking details and Cloud Voice usage, you can get an approximate calculation of the network requirements for your Cloud Voice deployment, manage and export these details for reporting, and view areas for further investigation and next steps.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-821">尽管网络规划人员不到网络规划人员输入网络信息后完全，自动生成映射过程它可以然后导出到构建文件供上载。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-821">Although the Network Planner doesn’t automate the building mapping process entirely, after network information is entered into the Network Planner it can then be exported to a building file ready for upload.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-822">我们强烈建议您利用网络规划人员，部署评估的总体影响在网络上的媒体工作负荷时。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-822">We highly recommend that you leverage the Network Planner when deploying media workloads on your network to assess the overall impact.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-823">有关网络计划工具的详细信息，请访问[MyAdvisor](https://myadvisor.fasttrack.microsoft.com/CloudVoice/NetworkPlanner)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-823">For more information about the Network Planner, visit [MyAdvisor](https://myadvisor.fasttrack.microsoft.com/CloudVoice/NetworkPlanner).</span></span>


## <a name="diagnostic-alerts"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-824">诊断通知</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-824">Diagnostic alerts</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-825">Microsoft 主动监视 CQD 遥测创建有关产生负面影响的用户体验的已知问题的诊断通知。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-825">Microsoft proactively monitors CQD telemetry to create diagnostic alerts for known issues that negatively affect the user experience.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-826">这些通知自动然后送达消息中心通过服务管理员。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-826">These alerts are then automatically delivered to the service administrator via the message center.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-827">下表概括了诊断消息中心，以及指向详细信息中显示的通知。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-827">The following table outlines the diagnostic alerts that are shown in the message center, along with links to more information.</span></span>

### <a name="message-center"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-845">消息中心</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-845">Message center</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-846">邮件中心在警告您有关新的更新、 功能或问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-846">The message center alerts you about new updates, features, or issues.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-847">服务管理员在 Microsoft 365 管理中心中的可用邮件中心。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-847">The message center is available within the Microsoft 365 admin center to service administrators.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-848">每个文章提供了简要概述如何更新、 功能或问题影响您的用户，并提供更多详细信息的链接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-848">Each post provides a high-level overview of how the update, feature, or issue affects your users, and gives links to more detailed information.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-849">若要打开邮件中心中，在 Microsoft 365 管理中心，转到**运行状况** > **消息中心**或选择消息中心卡**主页**仪表板上。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-849">To open the message center, in the Microsoft 365 admin center, go to **Health** > **Message center**, or select the message center card on the **Home** dashboard.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-850">仪表板显示已发布的最后三个消息和链接到完整消息中心页。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-850">The dashboard displays the last three messages that were posted and links to the full message center page.</span></span>
 

![消息中心卡片显示已发布的最后三个消息](media/qerguide-image-messagecentercard.png)

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-852">_图 18-消息中心卡片_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-852">_Figure 18 - Message center card_</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-853">您可以使用移动设备上的[Office 365 管理应用程序](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?linkid=627216)以查看邮件中心，即了解最新的推送通知的好方法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-853">You can also use the [Office 365 Admin app](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?linkid=627216) on your mobile device to view the message center, which is a great way to stay current with push notifications.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-854">有关详细信息，请参阅[这篇文章](https://support.office.com/article/Message-center-in-Office-365-38FB3333-BFCC-4340-A37B-DEDA509C2093)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-854">For more information, see [this article](https://support.office.com/article/Message-center-in-Office-365-38FB3333-BFCC-4340-A37B-DEDA509C2093).</span></span>

## <a name="reliability-investigations"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-855">可靠性调查</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-855">Reliability investigations</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-856">提高质量的第一步是在组织内评估可靠性的状态。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-856">The first step to improving quality is to assess the state of reliability across the organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-857">可靠性至关重要良好的用户体验，因为我们开始测量可靠性的两个组件：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-857">Because reliability is vital to a positive user experience, we start with the two components that measure reliability:</span></span>

1.  <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-858">**安装失败：** 无法建立呼叫。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-858">**Setup failures:** The call couldn’t be established.</span></span>

2.  <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-859">**放置失败：** 建立和意外终止呼叫。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-859">**Drop failures:** The call was established and unexpectedly terminated.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-860">整个此部分中，我们将介绍方法来进行调查这两个区域。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-860">Throughout this section, we’ll cover methods to investigate both areas.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-861">在本指南中介绍的模板中包含的不是所有报告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-861">Not all reports included in the templates are covered in this guide.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-862">但是，如下所述的调查的方法仍适用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-862">However, the methods of investigation explained below still apply.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-863">请参阅单个报表说明的详细信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-863">Please refer to the individual report description for more information.</span></span>


### <a name="setup-failures"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-864">安装失败</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-864">Setup failures</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-865">优先此区域中的补救安装失败，因为这些失败的用户体验产生重大负面影响。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-865">Prioritize remediating setup failures in this area first, because these failures have a significant negative impact on the user experience.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-866">首先调查评估组织的总体安装失败的百分比，然后设置其优先级的调查基于最高的百分比构建或网络区域。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-866">Begin your investigation by assessing the percentage of overall setup failures for the organization, and then prioritize areas of investigation based on the highest percentage by building or network.</span></span> 

#### <a name="setup-failure-trend-analysis"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-867">安装失败趋势分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-867">Setup failure trend analysis</span></span>

##### <a name="analysis"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-872">分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-872">Analysis</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-873">通过使用此报告，您可以回答以下问题和确定您的操作的下一过程：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-873">By using this report, you can answer the following questions and determine your next course of action:</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-874">什么是当前月份的总呼叫安装失败百分比？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-874">What is the total call setup failure percentage for the current month?</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-875">是总呼叫安装失败百分比低于或高于定义的目标指标？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-875">Is the total call setup failure percentage below or above the defined target metric?</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-876">严重或优于上个月是故障趋势？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-876">Is the failure trend worse or better than the previous month?</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-877">故障趋势增加，steady，或减少？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-877">Is the failure trend increasing, steady, or decreasing?</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-878">以前的解答，不管花时间来进行调查进一步使用辅助子报表以查找任何单个建筑或可能需要修复的子网。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-878">Irrespective of the previous answers, take the time to investigate further by using the companion sub-reports to look for any individual buildings or subnets that might need remediation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-879">尽管总体失败率可能是下面目标指标，对于一个或多个建筑或网络故障率可能上方目标指标，需要进行调查。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-879">Although the overall failure rate might be below the target metric, the failure rates for one or more buildings or networks might be above the target metric and need investigation.</span></span>

#### <a name="setup-failure-investigations"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-880">安装失败调查</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-880">Setup failure investigations</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-881">此摘要报告用于发现并隔离任何建筑或可能需要修复的网络。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-881">This summary report is used to discover and isolate any buildings or networks that might need remediation.</span></span>
