##### <a name="diagnostic-alert"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-886">诊断通知</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-886">Diagnostic alert</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-887">如果您收到"限制在防火墙中的导致呼叫安装失败"呼叫安装失败，导致深度数据包检查"关注修复措施那些诊断通知首先确定子网。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-887">If you received a diagnostic alert “Restrictions in the firewall are causing call setup failures” or “Deep packet inspection is causing call setup failures,” focus your remediation efforts on those identified subnets first.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-888">该通知已识别产生负面影响呼叫可靠性的子网。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-888">The alert has identified subnets that are negatively affecting call reliability.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-889">可以使用可靠性部分中找到的安装程序故障报告以帮助修复。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-889">You can use the Setup Failures reports found in the Reliability section to assist with the remediation.</span></span>

##### <a name="remediation"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-890">修正</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-890">Remediation</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-891">关注您建筑或子网已失败的最大卷上的第一个修复措施。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-891">Focus your first remediation efforts on buildings or subnets that have the largest volume of failures.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-892">这将最大限度地对用户体验的影响，并帮助快速减少组织的呼叫安装失败的速率。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-892">This will maximize impact on the user experience and help to quickly reduce the rate of organizational call setup failures.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-893">下表列出了由 CQD 报告的安装程序失败的两个原因。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-893">The following table lists the two reasons for setup failures as reported by CQD.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-894">_表 7 – 呼叫安装失败的原因_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-894">_Table 7 – Reasons for Call Setup Failures_</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-895">调用安装失败原因</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-895">Call Setup Failures reason</span></span>       | <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-896">典型的原因</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-896">Typical cause</span></span>                    |
|----------------------------------|----------------------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-897">缺少 FW 深入数据包检查例外规则</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-897">Missing FW Deep Packet Inspection Exemption Rule</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-898">指示沿路径的网络设备的建立由于深入包检查规则阻止的媒体路径。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-898">Indicates that network equipment along the path prevented the media path from being established due to deep packet inspection rules.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-899">这可能是因为未正确配置的防火墙规则。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-899">This is likely due to firewall rules not being correctly configured.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-900">在此方案中，TCP 握手成功，但未在 SSL 握手。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-900">In this scenario, the TCP handshake succeeded but the SSL handshake didn’t.</span></span>      |
| <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-901">缺少 FW IP 阻止例外规则</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-901">Missing FW IP Block Exception Rule</span></span>      | <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-902">指示沿路径的网络设备的建立到 Office 365 网络阻止的媒体路径。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-902">Indicates that network equipment along the path prevented the media path from being established to the Office 365 network.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-903">这可能是由于不允许访问 IP 地址和端口用于个团队和 Skype 业务通信正确配置代理服务器或防火墙规则。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-903">This might be due to proxy or firewall rules not being correctly configured to allow access to IP addresses and ports used for Teams and Skype for Business traffic.</span></span> |

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-904">现在您修正开始时，您可以将精力上特定构建或子网。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-904">Now as you begin your remediation, you can focus your efforts on a particular building or subnet.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-905">如前面的表所示，这些问题是由于防火墙或代理的配置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-905">As the preceding table shows, these issues are due to firewall or proxy configurations.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-906">查看修正操作下表中的选项。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-906">Review the options in the following table for remediation actions.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-907">_表 8-呼叫的后续步骤安装失败修正_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-907">_Table 8 - Next Steps for Call Setup Failure Remediation_</span></span>


|      <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-908">修正</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-908">Remediation</span></span>      |                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-909">指引</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-909">Guidance</span></span>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |
|-----------------------|----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-910">配置防火墙</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-910">Configure firewall(s)</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-911">与网络团队合作，并确认您针对[Office 365 IP 地址列表](https://aka.ms/o365ips)的防火墙配置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-911">Work with your network team and verify your firewall(s) configuration against [the Office 365 IP address list](https://aka.ms/o365ips).</span></span><br><br><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-912">确认的防火墙规则包含[媒体子网](https://support.office.com/article/Office-365-URLs-and-IP-address-ranges-8548a211-3fe7-47cb-abb1-355ea5aa88a2#bkmk_teams)和端口。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-912">Verify that the [media subnets](https://support.office.com/article/Office-365-URLs-and-IP-address-ranges-8548a211-3fe7-47cb-abb1-355ea5aa88a2#bkmk_teams) and ports are included in the firewall rules.</span></span> <br><br><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-913">验证在防火墙中打开所需的端口 （如下所示）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-913">Verify that the necessary ports (listed below) are opened in the firewall.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-914">UDP 应该能得到优先级，因为 TCP 被视为音频、 视频、 故障回复协议和基于视频的屏幕共享，以及其使用会影响呼叫的质量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-914">UDP should be given priority because TCP is considered a failback protocol for audio, video, and video-based screen sharing, and its use will affect the quality of the call.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-915">旧 RDP 应用程序共享仅使用 TCP。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-915">Legacy RDP application sharing uses TCP only.</span></span><br><ul><li><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-916">**TCP:** 端口 443</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-916">**TCP:** port 443</span></span></li><li><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-917">**UDP:** 端口 3478 – 3481</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-917">**UDP:** ports 3478–3481</span></span></li><ul> |
|        <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-918">验证</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-918">Verify</span></span>         |                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-919">[Microsoft 网络评估工具](https://www.microsoft.com/download/details.aspx?id=53885)用于验证从受影响的构建或子网的连接使用连接检查函数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-919">Use the [Microsoft Network Assessment Tool](https://www.microsoft.com/download/details.aspx?id=53885) to verify connectivity from the affected building or subnet by using the connectivity check function.</span></span>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |

### <a name="drop-failures"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-920">Drop 失败</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-920">Drop failures</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-921">与安装程序故障代码不同 CDQ 具有以指示为什么投递出现故障，这样就变得比较困难隔离特定根源无投递故障代码。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-921">Unlike setup failure codes, CDQ has no drop failure code to indicate why drop failures occur, which makes it difficult to isolate a specific root cause.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-922">更好会审放置失败，请使用推测的方法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-922">To better triage drop failures, use an inferred approach.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-923">通过补救媒体、 修补客户端和驱动程序，感兴趣的任何区域和个团队和 Skype for Business 的认证设备的驱动使用情况，您可以预期拒绝投递失败。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-923">By remediating any areas of interest for media, patching clients and drivers, and driving usage of certified devices for Teams and Skype for Business, you can expect drop failures to decline.</span></span>

#### <a name="drop-failure-trend-analysis"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-924">Drop 失败趋势分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-924">Drop failure trend analysis</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-925">此报表显示音频流、 总投递故障和投递失败率的总量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-925">This report displays the total amount of audio streams, total drop failures, and the drop failure rate.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-926">指向要显示其值的列中的任何一个，如下图所示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-926">Point to any one of the columns to display its values, as shown in the following figure.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-930">通过使用此类型的报告，您可以回答以下问题：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-930">By using this type of report, you can answer the following questions:</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-931">什么是当前的投递失败率？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-931">What is the current drop failure rate?</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-932">投递失败率低于定义的目标指标？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-932">Is the drop failure rate below the defined target metric?</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-933">严重或优于上个月是故障趋势？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-933">Is the failure trend worse or better than the previous month?</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-934">故障趋势增加，steady，或减少？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-934">Is the failure trend increasing, steady, or decreasing?</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-935">不管上面的问题的答案花时间来进行调查使用子报表以查找任何建筑或可能需要修复的网络。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-935">Irrespective of the answers to the questions above, take the time to investigate using the sub-reports to look for any buildings or networks that might need remediation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-936">尽管总体投递故障率可能是下面目标指标，投递失败率的一个或多个建筑或网络可能是上方目标指标，并且需要调查。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-936">Although the overall drop failure rate might be below the target metric, the drop failure rate for one or more buildings or networks might be above the target metric and need investigation.</span></span>

#### <a name="drop-failure-investigations"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-937">Drop 故障调查</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-937">Drop failure investigations</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-938">故障这里报告指示呼叫已被意外删除，并导致负用户体验。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-938">Failures reported here indicate that the call was dropped unexpectedly and resulted in a negative user experience.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-939">与不同趋势报告，这些报告提供其他见解需要进一步调查的特定子网。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-939">Unlike the trending reports, these reports provide additional insights into specific subnets that need further investigation.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-943">_图 22 – 按子网的投递失败_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-943">_Figure 22 – Drop failures by subnet_</span></span>

##### <a name="remediation"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-944">修正</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-944">Remediation</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-945">使用包含的表报表，您可以隔离网络中的区域的投递速率所在上方的目标指标您已定义的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-945">Using the included table reports, you can isolate problem areas in the network where the drop rate is above the target metric you’ve defined.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-946">关注您建筑或具有最高的总流计数，以便最大的影响的子网上的第一个修复措施。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-946">Focus your first remediation efforts on buildings or subnets that have the highest total stream count, to make the biggest impact.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-947">呼叫下降的常见原因：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-947">Common causes of call drops:</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-948">下设置网络或 internet 出口</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-948">Under-provisioned network or internet egress</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-949">配置受约束的网络上没有 QoS</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-949">No QoS configured on constrained networks</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-950">旧客户端版本</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-950">Older client versions</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-951">用户行为</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-951">User behavior</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-952">发现问题区域后，您可以使用[调用分析](https://techcommunity.microsoft.com/t5/Skype-for-Business-Blog/Introducing-Call-Analytics/ba-p/57309)进一步查看该生成的具体问题中的用户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-952">After you discover your problem areas, you can use [Call Analytics](https://techcommunity.microsoft.com/t5/Skype-for-Business-Blog/Introducing-Call-Analytics/ba-p/57309) to further review users in that building for specific issues.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-953">呼叫分析包含 PII 数据，可用于进一步隔离投递故障的可能原因。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-953">Call Analytics contains PII data and can be useful for further isolating potential reasons for the drop failures.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-954">无论您下一步，最好通知帮助台已与特定建筑或子网发现的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-954">Regardless of your next step, it’s a good practice to notify the helpdesk that an issue has been discovered with specific buildings or subnets.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-955">这种方式，可以快速地响应传入呼叫并更有效地会审用户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-955">This way, they can quickly respond to incoming calls and triage users more efficiently.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-956">然后可以向工程团队进行进一步调查后报告已标记的用户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-956">Flagged users can then be reported back to the engineering team for further investigation.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-957">下表列出了一些常见方法管理和修正投递失败。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-957">The following table lists some common methods to manage and remediate drop failures.</span></span>

data-ttu-id="d5b37-962">**拥塞**： 使用您的网络团队监视在特定建筑物/子网确认不存在问题与过度使用带宽。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-962">**Congestion**: Work with your network team to monitor bandwidth at 如何应对带宽和网络发生更改，以及建议个团队和 Skype for Business 的网络的做法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-971">**Perform a network readiness assessment**: A network assessment provides details about | <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-984">**用户行为**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-984">**User behavior**</span></span>                            | <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-985">如果您确定，既未网络、 设备或客户端问题，请考虑[我顾问](https://aka.ms/myadvisor)适当的开发培训用户如何以最佳加入并退出会议的用户应用策略的指南。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-985">If you determine that neither network, devices, or clients are the issue, consider engaging [My Advisor](https://aka.ms/myadvisor)  for guidance in developing a user adoption strategy to educate users how to best join and exit meetings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-986">效率团队和业务用户的 Skype 将会议中的所有参与者的用于生成更好的用户体验。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-986">A smarter Teams and Skype for Business user will produce a better user experience for all participants in the meeting.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-987">将其便携式计算机置入休眠模式 （通过关闭盖） 放而不退出会议的用户将被分类为意外的调用投递。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-987">A user who puts their laptop to sleep (by closing the lid) without exiting the meeting will be classified as an unexpected call drop.</span></span>   |

## <a name="quality-investigations"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-988">质量调查</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-988">Quality investigations</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-989">评估组织内的音频质量的状态下一步是调查差流率 (PSR)、 TCP 和代理使用率。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-989">The next step to assess the state of audio quality across the organization is to investigate Poor Stream Rate (PSR), TCP, and proxy usage.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-990">务必要记住 CQD 数据不提供具体的根本原因，但您改用提供可能的问题的区域以开始使用修正活动的相应团队协作会话。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-990">It’s important to remember that CQD data doesn’t provide you a specific root cause, but instead provides you with likely problem areas to begin a collaborative conversation with the appropriate teams for remediation activities.</span></span> 

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-991">在本指南; 中介绍的模板中包含的不是所有报告但是，这些报告仍适用调查如下所述的方法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-991">Not all reports included in the templates are covered in this guide; however, the methods of investigation explained below will still apply for those reports.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-992">引用的详细信息的单个报表说明。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-992">Refer to the individual report description for more information.</span></span> 

### <a name="quality"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-993">质量</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-993">Quality</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-994">PSR 百分比用于指示组织是否会议给定的焦点区域定义度量的目标。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-994">The PSR percentages are used to indicate whether the organization is meeting defined metric targets for a given focus area.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-995">请务必注意，即使高级百分比中定义的目标，单个子网或建筑可能不满足定义的目标，因此，需要进一步调查。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-995">It’s important to note that even if the high-level percentages are within the defined target, individual subnets or buildings might not meet the defined targets and, therefore, need further investigation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-996">例如，如果总体音频 PSR 百分比中 2 %april、 满足示例目标、 单个建筑物和子网可能仍存在不佳的体验，具体取决于该 2%的总体分布。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-996">For example, if the overall audio PSR percentage is 2 percent in April, which meets the sample target, individual buildings and subnets might still be having poor experiences, depending on the overall distribution of that 2 percent.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-997">若要评估差流的百分比，请使用质量报告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-997">To assess the percentage of poor streams, use the quality reports.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-998">提供了各种质量报告以查看 PSTN 呼叫，VPN 和会议室的总体，会议，两方的指标。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-998">Various quality reports are provided to review metrics for overall, conferencing, two-party, PSTN calling, VPN, and meeting rooms.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-999">每月、 每周和每日报告提供可帮助完成此过程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-999">Monthly, weekly, and daily reports are provided to assist in this process.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1000">每周和每日报告仅限于托管网络模板以提高其效率并降低干扰。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1000">Weekly and daily reports are limited to the Managed Networks template to increase their effectiveness and reduce noise.</span></span> 

#### <a name="quality-trend-analysis"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1001">质量趋势分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1001">Quality trend analysis</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1002">趋势报告显示随着时间的推移质量信息和用于帮助确定并了解感兴趣的每个区域内的质量趋势。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1002">Trending reports display quality information over time and are used to help identify and understand quality trends within each area of interest.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1003">如上所述，有对于调查质量; 模板中包括的报表树会议、 双方、 PSTN 呼叫、 VPN 和会议室。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1003">As noted above, there are report trees included in the templates for investigating quality; conferencing, two-party, PSTN calling, VPN, and meeting rooms.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1004">为了分析质量，调查过程是相同的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1004">For the purposes of analyzing quality, the investigative process is the same.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1005">但是，我们建议首先，开始会议因为会议质量中的任何改进还产生积极将影响所有其他区域。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1005">However, we recommend that you start with conferencing first, because any improvements in conference quality will also positively affect all other areas.</span></span> 

> [!Note]
> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1006">调查两方 （英文）、 PSTN 电话和会议室是类似于调查会议。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1006">Investigating two-party, PSTN calling, and meeting rooms are similar to investigating conferencing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1007">Focus 是到 isloate 建筑或子网已坏的质量并确定质量不佳的原因。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1007">The focus is to isloate buildings or subnets that have the worst quality and identify the reason for the poor quality.</span></span>

> [!Important]
> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1008">使用第二个 VPN 维度筛选基于 VPN 的报表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1008">VPN-based reports are filtered by using the Second VPN dimension.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1009">此维度需要 VPN 网络适配器正确注册为远程访问适配器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1009">This dimension requires that the VPN network adapter be properly registered as a Remote Access Adapter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1010">VPN 供应商不可靠地使用此标志，并且您里程将取决于在您的组织部署 VPN 供应商。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1010">VPN vendors don’t reliably use this flag, and your mileage will vary depending on the VPN vendor deployed at your organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1011">请遵循分级显示[本指南上文中](#vpn)修改 VPN 报告在需要时使用的构建或网络名称的指南。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1011">Follow the guidance outlined [earlier in this guide](#vpn) for modifying the VPN reports if needed by using the building or network name.</span></span>

![显示的质量不佳流百分比的图表](media/qerguide-image-audioqualityconferencing.png)

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1013">_图 23 – 音频质量-会议_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1013">_Figure 23 – Audio Quality - Conferencing_</span></span>

##### <a name="investigation"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1014">调查</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1014">Investigation</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1015">通过使用这些报告，您可以回答以下问题：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1015">By using these reports, you can answer the following questions:</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1016">什么是当前月份的总 PSR？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1016">What is the total PSR for the current month?</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1017">PSR 低于定义的目标指标？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1017">Is the PSR below the defined target metric?</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1018">严重或优于上个月是 PSR？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1018">Is PSR worse or better than the previous month?</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1019">PSR 趋势增加，steady，或减少？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1019">Is the PSR trend increasing, steady, or decreasing?</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1020">对上述，问题的解答不管花时间使用子报表以查找任何建筑或子网可能需要调查调查。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1020">Irrespective of the answers to the questions above, take the time to investigate by using the sub-reports to look for any buildings or subnets that might need investigation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1021">尽管总体 PSR 可能是下面目标指标，通常为一个或多个建筑或网络 PSR 超过指标，并且需要修复。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1021">Although the overall PSR might be below the target metric, often the PSR for one or more buildings or networks is above the metric and needs remediation.</span></span>

#### <a name="quality-investigations"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1022">质量调查</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1022">Quality investigations</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1023">质量摘要报告为您提供更深入的见解到什么全球分配到的流的被分类为质量欠佳，并有助于隔离中托管网络问题区域。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1023">The quality summary reports give you deeper insight into what contributed to the streams’ being classified as poor and helps to isolate problem areas in the managed network.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1024">虽然使用的维度可能会稍有不同之间报告，每个报告将包含总流数、 总差流、 PSR 和 0: 质量不佳的度量单位。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1024">Although the dimensions used might differ slightly between report, each report will include measures for total streams, total poor streams, PSR, and poor quality due to.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1025">已为感兴趣的每个区域创建报告： 会议，两方 PSTN 呼叫，VPN 和会议聊天室。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1025">Reports have been created for each area of interest: conferencing, two-party, PSTN calling, VPN, and meeting rooms.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1026">管理网络模板包括附加报告利用上载通过生成文件的位置信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1026">The Managed Network template includes additional reports to take advantage of the location information uploaded via the building file.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1027">请务必调整到当前月份月年筛选器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1027">Be sure to adjust the Month Year filter to the current month.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1028">选择**编辑**，然后调整**月年**保存新默认的月份。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1028">Select **Edit**, and adjust **Month Year** to save the new default month.</span></span>

> [!Note]
> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1029">常见的子网难以会审由于其广泛使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1029">Common subnets are difficult to triage due to their widespread use.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1030">已添加到所有网络模板，用于帮助解决使用常见的网络的机构与单独的报告显示客户端的公共 IP (第二个身本地 IP)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1030">A separate report that displays the client’s public IP (Second Reflexive Local IP) has been added to the All Networks template to assist with remediating offices that use common networks.</span></span>

##### <a name="diagnostic-alert"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1033">诊断通知</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1033">Diagnostic alert</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1034">如果您收到诊断警报"Wi-fi 网络上的会议室内设备导致质量欠佳的呼叫质量"包括和在您的修复措施设置这些设备的优先级。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1034">If you received a diagnostic alert “Meeting room devices on Wi-Fi networks are causing poor call quality,” include and prioritize those devices in your remediation efforts.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1035">该通知已识别主动导致质量欠佳的呼叫质量的会议室，Wi-fi 上。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1035">The alert has identified meeting rooms on Wi-Fi that are actively contributing to poor call quality.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1036">如果您收到诊断警报"VPN 使用率影响呼叫质量"调查拆分隧道的解决方案，以绕过 VPN 设备，允许媒体直接连接到服务。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1036">If you receive a diagnostic alert “VPN usage is affecting call quality,” investigate a split-tunneling solution to bypass the VPN appliance and allow media to directly connect to the service.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1037">该通知已识别 VPN 产生负面影响呼叫质量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1037">The alert has identified that VPN is negatively affecting call quality.</span></span>

##### <a name="remediation"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1038">修正</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1038">Remediation</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1039">关注您建筑或具有的最大流，量，因为这将最大限度地影响，并帮助改善用户体验快速的子网的修复措施。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1039">Focus your remediation efforts on buildings or subnets that have the largest volume of streams, because this will maximize impact and help to improve the user experience quickly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1040">使用抖动、 数据包丢失和往返时间 (RTT) 度量了解什么分配给质量不佳 （它是可能有多个问题）：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1040">Use the jitter, packet loss, and round-trip time (RTT) measurements to understand what’s contributing to the poor quality (it’s possible for there to be more than one problem):</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1041">**抖动**： 媒体数据包到达以不同的速度，从而导致扬声器发出声音自动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1041">**Jitter**: Media packets are arriving at different speeds, which causes a speaker to sound robotic.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1042">**数据包丢失**： 媒体数据包将被丢弃，这将创建缺少的单词或音节的影响。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1042">**Packet loss**: Media packets are being dropped, which creates the effect of missing words or syllables.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1043">**RTT**： 媒体数据包正在获取其目标，创建一个 walkie-talkie 效果很长时间。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1043">**RTT**: Media packets are taking a long time to get to their destination, which creates a walkie-talkie effect.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1044">为了帮助您研究质量问题，您可以利用[呼叫分析](https://techcommunity.microsoft.com/t5/Skype-for-Business-Blog/Introducing-Call-Analytics/ba-p/57309)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1044">To assist your investigation into quality issues, you can leverage [Call Analytics](https://techcommunity.microsoft.com/t5/Skype-for-Business-Blog/Introducing-Call-Analytics/ba-p/57309).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1045">使用呼叫分析，您可以查看特定会议或用户的详细的呼叫报告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1045">With Call Analytics, you can look at a specific conference or users’ detailed call report.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1046">此报告将包含 PII 数据，正在寻找失败的原因时很有用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1046">This report will contain PII data and is useful when you’re looking for the cause of a failure.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1047">您知道受影响的构建后，它应简单跟踪该构建中的用户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1047">After you know which building is affected, it should be straightforward to track down users in that building.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1048">不要忘记让支持人员了解这些网络遇到质量问题，以便他们可以快速会审并响应传入呼叫。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1048">Don’t forget to let the helpdesk know that these networks are experiencing quality issues, so they can quickly triage and respond to incoming calls.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1049">_表 10-常见贡献高 PSR_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1049">_Table 10 - Common contributors to high PSR_</span></span>

media quality.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1054">使用网络团队核实，确定是否从用户网络连接到 internet 出口点具有足够的带宽来支持媒体。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1054">Work with the network team to Planner](https://myadvisor.fasttrack.microsoft.com/CloudVoice/NetworkPlanner) can help you better understand your organization’s bandwidth needs.</span></span><br><br><span readiness assessment**: A network assessment provides details about expected bandwidth usage, how to cope with bandwidth and network changes, and recommended networking practices for Teams and Skype for Business.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1057">使用上表作为您的源，必须建筑或子网的最佳候选人评估的列表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1057">Using the preceding table as your source, you have a list of buildings or subnets that are excellent candidates for an assessment.</span></span><ul><li>[<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1058">Microsoft 团队网络准备情况评估</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span Assessment</span></span>](https://myadvisor.fasttrack.microsoft.com/CloudVoice/Offers/?pageState=NetworkReadiness)</li></ul><br><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1060">**Microsoft 网络评估工具：** to determine how well the network would perform for a Teams or Skype for Business Online call.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1061">此工具可帮助您评估子网的性能和验证针对 Microsoft | <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1063">**服务质量 (QoS)**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1063">**Quality of Service (QoS)**</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1064">QoS 是该经验证的工具，可帮助确定优先级数据包拥塞的网络，以确保它们到达其保持不变的目标和时间。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1064">QoS is a proven tool to help prioritize packets on a congested network to ensure they arrive at their destination intact and on time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1065">请考虑实现跨组织最大限度地受到限制带宽，其中的用户体验质量的 QoS。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1065">Consider implementing QoS across your organization to maximize the quality of the user experience where bandwidth is constrained.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1066">QoS 将帮助您解决通常与数据包丢失的高级别关联的问题和 — 在较小者一定程度上 — 不稳定和往返行程的时间。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1066">QoS will help solve issues typically associated with high levels of packet loss, and—to a lesser degree—jitter and round-trip times.</span></span><ul><li>[<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1067">Microsoft 团队 QoS 指南</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1067">Microsoft Teams QoS guidance</span></span>](qos-in-teams.md)</li><li>[<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1068">Skype 的业务 QoS 指南</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1068">Skype for Business QoS guidance</span></span>](https://myadvisor.fasttrack.microsoft.com/CloudVoice/Downloads?SelectedIDs=5_1_0_8)</li></ul> |
| <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1069">**Wi-Fi**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1069">**Wi-Fi**</span></span>               | <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1070">Wi-fi 可以对呼叫质量产生重大影响。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1070">Wi-Fi can have a significant impact on call quality.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1071">Wi-fi 部署不通常考虑 VoIP 服务的网络要求，而且通常质量不佳的源。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1071">Wi-Fi deployments don’t typically take into consideration the network requirements for VoIP services and are often a source of poor quality.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1072">有关优化 Wi-fi 基础结构的详细信息，请参阅[关于 Wi-fi 规划这篇文章](/skypeforbusiness/certification/plan-wifi)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1072">For more information about optimizing your Wi-Fi infrastructure, see [this article about Wi-Fi planning](/skypeforbusiness/certification/plan-wifi).</span></span><br><br><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1073">**无线驱动程序**： 确保无线驱动因素保持最新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1073">**Wireless driver**: Ensure that wireless drivers are up to date.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1074">这有助于减轻任何用户体验不佳与过期的驱动程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1074">This will help mitigate any poor user experience related to an outdated driver.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1075">许多组织不在其修补程序周期中，包括无线驱动程序和年这些驱动程序可以转未安装修补程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1075">Many organizations don’t include wireless drivers in their patch cycles, and these drivers can go unpatched for years.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1076">通过确保无线驱动程序最新解决了许多无线问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1076">Many wireless issues are solved by ensuring the wireless drivers are up to date.</span></span><br><br><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1077">**WMM**： 无线多媒体扩展 (WMM)，也称为 Wi-fi 多媒体，提供了到无线网络的基本 QoS 功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1077">**WMM**: Wireless Multimedia Extensions (WMM), also known as Wi-Fi Multimedia, provides basic QoS features to wireless networks.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1078">现代无线网络必须支持多个设备。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1078">Modern wireless networks must support many devices.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1079">这些设备争夺带宽，并可能导致 VoIP 服务的质量问题的速度和延迟至关重要。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1079">These devices compete for bandwidth and can lead to quality issues for VoIP services, where speed and latency are vital.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1080">咨询您的无线供应商的详细信息，并考虑实现对您的无线网络，若要设置业务和团队媒体的 Skype WMM。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1080">Consult your wireless vendor for specifics and consider implementing WMM on your wireless network to prioritize Skype for Business and Teams media.</span></span><br><br><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1081">**访问点密度**： 访问点太可能远或不在的理想位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1081">**Access point density**: Access points might be too far apart or not in an ideal location.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1082">大程度地减少潜在干扰，将额外访问点放在会议室和不受阻背景墙或其他对象的弱 Wi-fi 信号所在的位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1082">To minimize potential interference, place extra access points in conference rooms and in locations that aren’t obstructed by walls or other objects where the Wi-Fi signal is weak.</span></span><br><br><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1083">**与 5 GHz 2.4 GHz**: 5 GHz 提供较少的背景干扰和更高的速度，并通过 Wi-fi 部署 VoIP 时应确定优先级。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1083">**2.4 GHz versus 5 GHz**: 5 GHz provides less background interference and higher speeds, and should be prioritized when deploying VoIP over Wi-Fi.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1084">但是，5 GHz 不与 2.4 GHz 为强，并且不入侵轻松地的背景墙。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1084">However, 5 GHz isn’t as strong as 2.4 GHz and doesn’t penetrate walls as easily.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1085">查看您构建的布局来确定可以最佳的连接依赖的频率。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1085">Review your building layout to determine which frequency you can rely on for the best connection.</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1086">**网络设备**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1086">**Network device**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1087">较大的组织可能有数百个分散在网络设备。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1087">Larger organizations might have hundreds of devices spread out across the network.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1088">使用您的网络团队确保从用户到 internet 的网络设备的维护和最新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1088">Work with your network team to ensure that the network devices from the user to the internet are maintained and up to date.</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1089">**VPN**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1089">**VPN**</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1090">通常情况下，VPN 设备不旨在处理实时的媒体工作负荷。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1090">VPN appliances aren’t traditionally designed to handle real-time media workloads.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1091">某些 VPN 配置禁止使用 UDP （这是首选的协议媒体），并且仅依赖 TCP。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1091">Some VPN configurations prohibit the use of UDP (which is the preferred protocol for media) and rely on TCP only.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1092">请考虑实现[VPN 拆分隧道解决方案](https://myadvisor.fasttrack.microsoft.com/CloudVoice/Downloads?SelectedIDs=5_1_0_9)以帮助减少 VPN 作为质量不佳的一个来源。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1092">Consider implementing a [VPN split-tunnel solution](https://myadvisor.fasttrack.microsoft.com/CloudVoice/Downloads?SelectedIDs=5_1_0_9) to help reduce VPN as a source of poor quality.</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1093">**客户端**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1093">**Clients**</span></span> <br><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1094">(For Business 的 Skype 仅联机)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1094">(Skype for Business Online only)</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1095">具有已知旧版客户端与媒体造成问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1095">Older clients have been known to cause issues with media.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1096">确保客户端的版本的六个月内修补。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1096">Ensure that clients are being patched within six months of release.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1097">[MyAdvisor](https://aka.ms/myadvisor)用于开发的客户端准备策略的指南和部署[即点即单击](https://docs.microsoft.com/DeployOffice/deployment-guide-for-office-365-proplus)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1097">Use [MyAdvisor](https://aka.ms/myadvisor) for guidance on developing a client readiness strategy and deploy [Click-to-Run](https://docs.microsoft.com/DeployOffice/deployment-guide-for-office-365-proplus).</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1098">**Devices**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1098">**Devices**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1099">使用[优化设备](https://partnersolutions.skypeforbusiness.com/solutionscatalog)可以帮助明显改善用户体验。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1099">The use of [optimized devices](https://partnersolutions.skypeforbusiness.com/solutionscatalog) can help to significantly improve the user experience.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1100">与所有要素相同，优化的设备旨在最大限度地与团队业务的 Skype 的用户体验和生成出色的质量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1100">With all things being equal, optimized devices are designed to maximize the user experience with Teams and Skype for Business, and produce superior quality.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1101">[MyAdvisor](https://aka.ms/myadvisor)用于开发的设备准备策略的指南。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1101">Use [MyAdvisor](https://aka.ms/myadvisor) for guidance on developing a device readiness strategy.</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1102">**驱动程序**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1102">**Drivers**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1103">修补网络 （以太网和 Wi-fi） 音频、 视频和 USB 驱动程序应为总体修补程序管理策略的一部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1103">Patching network (Ethernet and Wi-Fi), audio, video, and USB drivers should be part of your overall patch management strategy.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1104">通过更新驱动程序解决了多个质量问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1104">Many quality issues are solved by updating drivers.</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1105">**Wi-fi 上的会议室**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1105">**Meeting rooms on Wi-Fi**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1106">我们强烈建议将会议的会议室设备连接到网络使用至少一个 1 Gbps 以太网连接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1106">We highly recommend that meeting room devices be connected to the network by using at least a 1-Gbps Ethernet connection.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1107">会议室内设备通常包括多个音频和视频流，以及会议内容，如屏幕共享，并具有更高版本与其他团队或 Skype 业务终结点的网络要求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1107">Meeting room devices typically include multiple audio and video streams, along with meeting content such as screen sharing, and have higher network requirements than other Teams or Skype for Business endpoints.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1108">会议室是，根据定义，信纸 Wi-fi 其中正好优点仅在安装过程中的设备。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1108">Meeting rooms are, by definition, stationary devices where Wi-Fi affords a benefit only during installation.</span></span><br><br><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1109">会议室需要额外的医护和采取行动，以确保使用这些设备的体验是满足或超过期望处理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1109">Meeting rooms need to be treated with extra care and attention to ensure that the experience using these devices is meeting or exceeding expectations.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1110">会议室质量问题通常要快速呈报因为高级员工通常正在使用它们。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1110">Quality issues with meeting rooms are usually going to be escalated quickly, because they’re often used by senior-level staff.</span></span><br><br><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1111">与所有要素相同 （除了方便），Wi-fi 性能通常小于有线连接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1111">With all things being equal (apart from convenience), Wi-Fi performance is often less than a wired connection.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1112">使用"使用您自己的设备"策略的上升和大量便携式计算机，常过度利用 Wi-fi 访问点。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1112">With the rise of “bring your own device” policies and the proliferation of laptops, Wi-Fi access points are often over-utilized.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1113">不可能在 Wi-fi 网络，这会导致在高峰使用质量问题划分优先级实时的媒体。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1113">Real-time media might not be prioritized on Wi-Fi networks, which can lead to quality issues during peak use times.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1114">此高强度使用情况可以与会议重合其中可能会出现一打人员出席，每个都有其自己的便携式计算机和智能手机连接到同一 Wi-fi 接入点作为会议的所有聊天室设备。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1114">This heavy usage can coincide with a meeting where there might be a dozen people in attendance, each with their own laptop and smartphone, all connected to the same Wi-Fi access point as the meeting room device.</span></span><br><br><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1115">Wi-fi 只应视为临时解决方案，对于移动安装，或已正确设置 Wi-fi 支持企业级、 基于现实时间媒体。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1115">Wi-Fi should only be considered as a temporary solution, for a mobile installation, or when Wi-Fi has been properly provisioned to support business-class, real-time–based media.</span></span> |


### <a name="tcp"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1116">TCP</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1116">TCP</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1117">故障回复传输和主要用于实时的媒体传输，将不被视为 TCP。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1117">TCP is considered a failback transport and not the primary transport you want for real-time media.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1118">它是一个故障回复传输的原因是 TCP 的性质状态。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1118">The reason it’s a failback transport is due to the stateful nature of TCP.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1119">例如，如果延迟网络上进行调用和延迟媒体数据包，然后从以前的几秒钟的数据包 — 不再有用的 — 争夺带宽，转到接收方，这会使错误情况变差。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1119">For example, if a call is made on a latent network and media packets are delayed, then packets from a few seconds ago—which are no longer useful—compete for bandwidth to get to the receiver, which can make a bad situation worse.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1120">这样的音频修复程序缝合和拉伸音频，导致听见项目，通常抖动形式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1120">This makes the audio healer stitch and stretch audio, resulting in audible artifacts, often in the form of jitter.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1121">本节中的报表不进行良好和差流之间的差异。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1121">The reports in this section don’t make a distinction between good and poor streams.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1122">UDP 是首选，报告将查找 TCP 用于音频、 视频和基于视频的屏幕共享 (VBSS)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1122">Given that UDP is preferred, the reports look for the use of TCP for audio, video, and video-based screen sharing (VBSS).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1123">提供了不佳流速率，以帮助比较 UDP 质量与 TCP 质量，以便您可以将精力其中影响是最大。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1123">Poor stream rates are provided to help compare UDP quality versus TCP quality so that you can focus your efforts where the impact is the greatest.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1124">TCP 使用的是主要原因： 未完成的防火墙规则。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1124">TCP usage is primarily caused by incomplete firewall rules.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1125">有关详细信息防火墙规则个团队和 Skype 业务 online，请参阅[Office 365 Url 和 IP 地址范围](https://aka.ms/o365ips)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1125">For more information about firewall rules for Teams and Skype for Business Online, see [Office 365 URLs and IP address ranges](https://aka.ms/o365ips).</span></span>

> [!Important]
> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1126">强烈建议具有[有效的生成文件](#building-mapping)上载，以便您可以快速区分内外部的流时看 TCP 使用率。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1126">Having a [valid building file](#building-mapping) uploaded is highly recommended so you can quickly distinguish inside from outside streams when looking at TCP usage.</span></span>

> [!Note]
> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1127">音频、 视频和 VBSS 所有首选 UDP 作为其主传输。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1127">Audio, video, and VBSS all prefer UDP as their primary transport.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1128">旧的 RDP 应用程序共享的工作负荷仅使用 TCP。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1128">The legacy RDP Application Sharing workload only uses TCP.</span></span>

#### <a name="tcp-usage"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1129">TCP 使用率</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1129">TCP usage</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1130">TCP 报告指示最近七个月的总体 TCP 使用情况。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1130">TCP reports indicates the overall TCP usage over the last seven months.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1131">本节中的所有进一步报告将重点缩小特定建筑和 TCP 最常使用的位置的子网。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1131">All further reports in this section will focus on narrowing down specific buildings and subnets where TCP is most commonly used.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1132">单独的报表供会议和两方流。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1132">Separate reports are available for both conferencing and two-party streams.</span></span>

##### <a name="investigation"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1134">调查</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1134">Investigation</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1135">通过使用此报告，您可以回答以下问题：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1135">By using this report, you can answer the following questions:</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1136">什么是当前月份的 TCP 流总量？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1136">What is the total volume of TCP streams for the current month?</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1137">很差或优于上个月？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1137">Is it worse or better than the previous month?</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1138">TCP 使用率趋势增加，steady，或减少？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1138">Is the TCP usage trend increasing, steady, or decreasing?</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1139">是 TCP PSR 我总体 PSR 相同？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1139">Is the TCP PSR the same as my overall PSR?</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1140">如果您注意到不断增加的 TCP 使用率趋势大于或等于每月的正常使用，需要使用子报表以查找任何建筑或网络可能需要修正调查时间。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1140">If you notice that the TCP usage trend is increasing or above normal monthly usage, take the time to investigate by using the sub-reports to look for any buildings or networks that might need remediation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1141">理想情况下，您希望托管网络上尽可能少 TCP 基于音频会话。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1141">Ideally, you want as few TCP-based audio sessions as possible on the managed network.</span></span>

#### <a name="tcp-vs-udp"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1142">TCP 和 UDP</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1142">TCP vs. UDP</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1143">此报表标识量 TCP 和 UDP 使用率报告的音频、 视频和基于视频的屏幕共享 (VBSS) 的最新月份。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1143">This report identifies the volume of TCP versus UDP usage reporting on the latest month for audio, video, and video-based screen sharing (VBSS).</span></span>

##### <a name="analysis"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1146">分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1146">Analysis</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1147">虽然您想要尽可能的低的 TCP 使用率，您可能会看到 TCP 用法，否则为正常部署中的位。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1147">Although you want TCP usage to be as low as possible, you might see a bit of TCP usage in an otherwise healthy deployment.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1148">TCP 本身不参与质量欠佳的呼叫，因此流率提供可帮助确定是否 TCP 使用率较质量不佳的贡献。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1148">TCP by itself won’t contribute to a poor call, so stream rates are provided to help identify whether TCP usage is a contributor to poor quality.</span></span> 

#### <a name="tcp-investigations"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1149">TCP 调查</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1149">TCP investigations</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1150">在提供 CQD 模板中，通过浏览到 TCP 流构建和子网报告使用的托管网络或所有网络的模板。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1150">In the provided CQD templates, navigate to the TCP Streams by Building and Subnet reports by using either the Managed Networks or All Networks template.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1151">调查 TCP 使用，以便过程是相同的因此我们将专注关于会议的讨论。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1151">For the purpose of investigating TCP usage, the process is the same, so we’ll focus the discussion here on conferencing.</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1152">有效[构建文件](#building-mapping)上载，建议以便您可以快速区分内外部的流时看 TCP 使用率。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1152">Having a valid [building file](#building-mapping) uploaded is recommended so you can quickly distinguish inside from outside streams when looking at TCP usage.</span></span> 

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1153">请务必调整到当前月份月年筛选器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1153">Be sure to adjust the Month Year filter to the current month.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1154">选择**编辑**，然后调整**月年**保存新默认的月份。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1154">Select **Edit**, and adjust **Month Year** to save the new default month.</span></span>                                  |

##### <a name="diagnostic-alert"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1157">诊断通知</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1157">Diagnostic alert</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1158">如果您收到诊断警报"UDP 通信限制，从而导致质量欠佳的呼叫质量"关注您 TCP 修复措施这些子网首先。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1158">If you received a diagnostic alert “UDP traffic is being limited, which causes poor call quality,” focus your TCP remediation efforts on those subnets first.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1159">该通知已识别其中使用 TCP 产生负面影响呼叫质量的子网。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1159">The alert has identified subnets where the use of TCP is negatively affecting call quality.</span></span>

##### <a name="remediation"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1160">修正</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1160">Remediation</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1161">此报表标识特定建筑和分配给 TCP 使用率量的子网。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1161">This report identifies specific buildings and subnets that are contributing to the volume of TCP usage.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1162">此外包含其他报表来标识呼叫中用来帮助隔离缺少防火墙规则 Microsoft 中继 IP。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1162">An additional report is also included to identify the Microsoft Relay IP that was used in the call to help isolate missing firewall rules.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1163">关注您在具有最高的 TCP 流以最大限度地影响音量这些建筑的修复措施。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1163">Focus your remediation efforts on those buildings that have the highest volume of TCP streams to maximize impact.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1164">TCP 使用率的最常见原因缺少在防火墙或代理的例外规则。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1164">The most common cause of TCP usage is missing exception rules in firewalls or proxies.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1165">我们将谈论代理的下一步部分，那么现在精力放在防火墙。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1165">We’ll be talking about proxies in the next section, so for now focus your efforts on the firewalls.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1166">通过使用构建或提供的子网，您可以确定哪些防火墙需要更新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1166">By using the building or subnet provided, you can determine which firewall needs to be updated.</span></span>


<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1167">_表 11-TCP 流构建和子网的补救指南_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1167">_Table 11 - Remediation guidance for TCP streams by building and subnet_</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1168">修正</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1168">Remediation</span></span>        | <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1169">指引</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1169">Guidance</span></span>     |
|--------------------|--------------------------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1170">配置防火墙</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1170">Configure firewall</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1171">验证[Office 365 IP 端口和地址](https://aka.ms/o365ips)会从您的防火墙中排除。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1171">Verify that [Office 365 IP ports and addresses](https://aka.ms/o365ips) are excluded from your firewall.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1172">有关媒体相关 TCP 问题，重点介绍您初始措施以下：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1172">For media-related TCP issues, focus your initial efforts on the following:</span></span><ul><li><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1173">验证客户端媒体的子网 13.107.64.0/18 和 52.112.0.0/14 位于防火墙规则。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1173">Verify that the client media subnets 13.107.64.0/18 and 52.112.0.0/14 are in your firewall rules.</span></span></li><li><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1174">UDP 3478 – 3481 端口是必需的媒体端口，且必须打开，否则将客户端故障回复到 TCP 端口 443。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1174">UDP ports 3478–3481 are the required media ports and must be opened, otherwise the client will fail back to TCP port 443.</span></span></li></ul> |
| <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1175">验证</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1175">Verify</span></span>             | <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1176">[Microsoft 网络评估工具](https://www.microsoft.com/download/details.aspx?id=53885)用于从受影响的构建或子网连接到特定的 Office 365 IP 地址和端口检查存在问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1176">Use the [Microsoft Network Assessment Tool](https://www.microsoft.com/download/details.aspx?id=53885) to check for issues with connectivity to specific Office 365 IP addresses and ports from the affected building or subnet.</span></span>    |

### <a name="http-proxy"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1177">HTTP 代理</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1177">HTTP proxy</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1178">HTTP 代理未建立媒体会话，用于军方的原因的首选的路径。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1178">HTTP proxies aren’t the preferred path for establishing media sessions, for a multitude of reasons.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1179">许多包含可以阻止连接到服务正在完成并引入缩至最短的深度数据包检查功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1179">Many contain deep packet inspection features that can prevent connections to the service from being completed and introduce disruptions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1180">此外，几乎所有代理而不是允许 UDP，最佳音频质量，建议都强制 TCP。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1180">Additionally, almost all proxies force TCP as opposed to allowing UDP, which is recommended for optimal audio quality.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1181">始终建议您配置客户端直接连接到工作组和 Skype 业务服务。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1181">We always recommend that you configure the client to directly connect to Teams and Skype for Business services.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1182">这一点尤其重要的基于媒体流量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1182">This is especially important for media-based traffic.</span></span>


> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1183">无有效[构建文件](#building-mapping)上载便于正确区分内外部的音频流在分析代理使用情况。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1183">Having a valid [building file](#building-mapping) uploaded makes it easy to properly distinguish inside from outside audio streams when analyzing proxy usage.</span></span> 


#### <a name="http-proxy-usage"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1184">使用 HTTP 代理</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1184">HTTP proxy usage</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1185">本节中的模板中的 HTTP 代理流报告很相似 TCP 报告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1185">The HTTP proxy stream report in this section of the template is much like the TCP reports.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1186">它看起来不在呼叫是否很差或良好，但呼叫是否已通过 HTTP 进行连接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1186">It doesn’t look at whether calls are poor or good, but whether the call is connected over HTTP.</span></span>

##### <a name="analysis"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1189">分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1189">Analysis</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1190">要查看为尽可能少的 HTTP 媒体流。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1190">You want to see as little HTTP media streams as possible.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1191">如果希望流遍历您的代理服务器，请咨询您的网络团队，以确保正确排除就地，以便客户端直接路由到团队或 Skype 而业务联机媒体子网。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1191">If you have streams traversing your proxy, consult your networking team to ensure that the proper exclusions are in place so that clients are directly routing to Teams or Skype for Business Online media subnets.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1192">如果已在组织中只有一个 internet 代理，确认正确的[Office 365 Url 和 IP 地址范围排除](https://aka.ms/o365ips)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1192">If you have only one internet proxy in your organization, verify the proper [Office 365 URLs and IP address range exclusions](https://aka.ms/o365ips).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1193">如果多个 internet 代理配置组织中使用 HTTP 子报告以隔离的构建或子网的影响。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1193">If more than one internet proxy is configured in your organization, use the HTTP sub-report to isolate which building or subnet is affected.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1194">无法绕过代理服务器，组织确保配置 Skype 业务客户端登录的正确时[一文中所述位于代理后面 for Business 的 Skype 应使用代理服务器而不是直接尝试登录连接](https://support.microsoft.com/help/3207112/skype-for-business-should-use-proxy-server-to-sign-in-instead-of-tryin)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1194">For organizations that can’t bypass the proxy, ensure that the Skype for Business client is configured to sign in properly when it’s located behind a proxy, as outlined in the article [Skype for Business should use proxy server to sign in instead of trying direct connection](https://support.microsoft.com/help/3207112/skype-for-business-should-use-proxy-server-to-sign-in-instead-of-tryin).</span></span> 


#### <a name="http-proxy-investigations"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1195">HTTP 代理调查</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1195">HTTP proxy investigations</span></span>

##### <a name="remediation"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1202">修正</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1202">Remediation</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1203">我们[建议](proxy-servers-for-skype-for-business-online.md)您始终绕的 Skype 代理过业务和团队，尤其是媒体流量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1203">We [recommend](proxy-servers-for-skype-for-business-online.md) that you always bypass proxies for Skype for Business and Teams, especially media traffic.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1204">代理不进行 for Business 的 Skype 更为安全，因为已对其流量进行加密。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1204">Proxies don't make Skype for Business more secure, because its traffic is already encrypted.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1205">环境中可能会出现由于延迟和数据包丢失而引起的与性能相关的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1205">Performance-related problems can be introduced to the environment through latency and packet loss.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1206">例如，这些问题将导致负体验，与音频、 视频和屏幕共享、 实时流至关重要。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1206">Issues such as these will result in a negative experience with audio, video and screen sharing, where real-time streams are essential.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1207">HTTP 使用率的最常见原因缺少中代理的例外规则。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1207">The most common cause of HTTP usage is missing exception rules in proxies.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1208">使用构建或子网，提供您可以快速确定哪些代理需要配置媒体绕过。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1208">By using the building or subnet provided, you can quickly determine which proxy needs to be configured for media bypass.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1209">确认所需的[Office 365 Fqdn](https://aka.ms/o365ips)白名单中您的代理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1209">Verify that the required [Office 365 FQDNs](https://aka.ms/o365ips) are whitelisted in your proxy.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1210">有关使用 Skype 业务联机和团队代理的详细信息，请参阅[这篇文章](proxy-servers-for-skype-for-business-online.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1210">For more information about using proxies with Skype for Business Online and Teams, see [this article](proxy-servers-for-skype-for-business-online.md).</span></span>

## <a name="endpoint-investigations"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1211">终结点调查</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1211">Endpoint investigations</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1212">本节重点介绍报告使用认证的设备和客户端版本的任务。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1212">This section is focused on the tasks for reporting on client versions and the use of certified devices.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1213">报告可供大纲使用率的客户端版本、 客户端类型、 捕获设备和驱动程序 （麦克风）、 视频捕获设备和 Wi-fi 供应商和驱动程序版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1213">Reports are available to outline usage for client versions, client type, capture devices and drivers (microphone), video capture devices, and Wi-Fi vendor and driver versions.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1214">在本指南; 中介绍的模板中包含的不是所有报告但是，如下所述的调查的方法仍适用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1214">Not all reports included in the templates are covered in this guide; however, the methods of investigation explained below still apply.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1215">引用的详细信息的单个报表说明。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1215">Refer to the individual report description for more information.</span></span>

### <a name="client-versions"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1216">客户端版本</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1216">Client versions</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1217">标识 Skype for Business 中使用的客户端版本与环境中的其相对批量重点此空间中的报表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1217">The reports in this space focus on identifying Skype for Business client versions in use and their relative volume in the environment.</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1218">目前，分发并自动更新通过 Azure 内容交付网络团队客户端和将保持最新的服务。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1218">Currently, Teams clients are distributed and updated automatically through the Azure Content Delivery Network and will be kept up to date by the service.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1219">客户端准备和调查活动不适用于团队。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1219">Client readiness and investigative activities aren’t applicable to Teams.</span></span>

> [!Important]
> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1220">除非您排除联盟参与者数据，这些报表将包括来自联盟的终结点的客户端遥测。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1220">Unless you exclude federated participant data, these reports will include client telemetry from federated endpoints.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1221">若要排除联盟的终结点，您必须添加第二个租户 ID 设置为贵组织的[租户 ID](#tenant-id)[查询筛选器](#query-filters)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1221">To exclude federated endpoints, you must add a [query filter](#query-filters) for Second Tenant ID set to your organization’s [tenant ID](#tenant-id).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1222">此外，您可以使用[URL 筛选器](#url-filter)中排除联盟参与者遥测。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1222">Alternatively, you can use a [URL filter](#url-filter) to exclude federated participant telemetry.</span></span>

#### <a name="diagnostic-alert"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1227">诊断通知</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1227">Diagnostic alert</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1228">如果收到诊断警报"客户端版本不佳的已知正在使用"功能，重点关注首次更新这些客户端。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1228">If you received a diagnostic alert ”Known poorly performing client versions are in use,” focus on updating those clients first.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1229">确定了这些客户端产生负面影响呼叫质量的通知。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1229">The alert has identified that these clients are negatively affecting your call quality.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1230">您可以使用客户端 & （如上所示） 以帮助确保不再更新具有已知问题的客户端设备报告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1230">You can use the Client & Devices report (shown above) to help ensure that the clients that have known issues are no longer being updated.</span></span>

#### <a name="remediation"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1231">修正</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1231">Remediation</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1232">托管客户端运行最新版本的 Skype for Business，除了确保支持音频、 视频、 网络和 USB 驱动程序是最新，确保驱动的高品质用户体验的关键部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1232">A critical part of driving high-quality user experiences is ensuring that managed clients are running up-to-date versions of Skype for Business, in addition to ensuring the supporting audio, video, network, and USB drivers are up to date.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1233">这可以提供有许多益处，其中包括：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1233">This provides several benefits, among them:</span></span> 

-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1234">很方便地管理与多个版本的几个版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1234">It’s easier to manage a few versions versus many versions.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1235">它提供了体验的一致性级别。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1235">It provides a level of consistency of experience.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1236">它可更轻松地解决问题呼叫质量和可用性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1236">It makes it easier to troubleshoot problems with call quality and usability.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1237">Microsoft 不断会使跨产品的常规改进和优化。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1237">Microsoft continually makes general improvements and optimizations across the product.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1238">确保用户接收这些更新减少了运行到已解决的问题的风险。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1238">Ensuring that users receive these updates reduces their risk of running into a problem that has already been solved.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1239">限制对客户端版本不超过六个月的部署将改进的整体用户体验，并减少需要支持的版本数量，从而提高可管理性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1239">Limiting your deployment to client versions that are less than six months old will improve the overall user experience and improve manageability by reducing the number of versions that need to be supported.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1240">如果您正在使用仅 Office 单击即点即，您将自动是六个月的时段内。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1240">If you’re using only Office Click-to-Run, you’ll automatically be within the six-month window.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1241">不不需要任何进一步的操作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1241">No further action is required.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1242">如果您具有单击即点即用的组合和安装程序包 (MSI)，您可以使用报表以验证定期更新 MSI 客户端。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1242">If you have a mix of Click-to-Run and installer packages (MSI), you can use the report to verify that the MSI clients are being updated regularly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1243">如果您注意到客户端落后，使用团队负责管理 Office 更新，并确保您批准并定期部署客户端修补程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1243">If you notice clients are falling behind, work with the team responsible for managing Office updates and ensure that they’re approving and deploying client patches regularly.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1244">也很重要考虑并确保网络，视频、 USB 和音频驱动程序修补以及。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1244">It’s also important to consider and ensure that the network, video, USB, and audio drivers are being patched as well.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1245">它可以轻松地忽略这些驱动程序并不包括在您的修补程序的管理策略。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1245">It can be easy to overlook these drivers and not include them in your patch management strategy.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1246">通过以下链接可找到 for Business 的 Skype 的版本号：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1246">Version numbers for Skype for Business can be found via the links below:</span></span>

-   [<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1247">发布的更新 Office ProPlus 的信息</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1247">Release information for updates to Office ProPlus</span></span>](https://docs.microsoft.com/officeupdates/release-notes-office365-proplus)
-   [<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1248">Office 365 ProPlus 的更新历史记录</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1248">Update history for Office 365 ProPlus</span></span>](https://docs.microsoft.com/officeupdates/update-history-office365-proplus-by-date)
