### <a name="devices"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1250">设备</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1250">Devices</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1251">若要使麦克风设备报告的使用，我们需要了解的意见得分概念 (MOS)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1251">To make use of the microphone device report, we need to understand the concept of the mean opinion score (MOS).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1252">MOS 是以衡量检测音频质量的金色标准度量值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1252">MOS is the gold-standard measurement to gauge the perceived audio quality.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1253">它表示为从 0 到 5 的整数分级。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1253">It’s represented as an integer rating from 0 to 5.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1254">语音质量的所有度量值的基础是人员可以语音质量的体验。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1254">The basis of all measures of voice quality is how a person perceives the quality of speech.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1255">它受 human 认知，因为它是本质上是主观。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1255">Because it’s affected by human perception, it’s inherently subjective.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1256">有几个不同的方法，用于主观测试。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1256">There are several different methodologies for subjective testing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1257">大多数语音质量度量值基于绝对分类评估 (ACR) 范围。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1257">Most voice quality measures are based on an absolute categorization rating (ACR) scale.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1258">在 ACR 主观测试中，统计大量人员评级其用户体验质量的范围为 1 （错误） 为 5 （极好）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1258">In an ACR subjective test, a statistically significant number of people rate their quality of experience on a scale of 1 (bad) to 5 (excellent).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1259">MOS 得分的平均值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1259">The average of the scores is the MOS.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1260">生成 MOS 取决于已公开到组中，为正在分级的体验的类型的体验的范围。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1260">The resulting MOS depends on the range of experiences that were exposed to the group and to the type of experience being rated.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1261">是不切实际进行实时通信系统的语音质量主观测试，因为 Microsoft 团队和 Skype for Business 使用高级的算法客观地预测主观测试的结果生成 MOS 值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1261">Because it’s impractical to conduct subjective tests of voice quality for a live communication system, Microsoft Teams and Skype for Business generate MOS values by using advanced algorithms to objectively predict the results of a subjective test.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1262">提供一组的 MOS 和关联的指标提供到传递给用户的音频设备的用户体验质量视图。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1262">The available set of MOS and associated metrics provide a view into the quality of the experience being delivered to the users by an audio device.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1263">通过为用户提供认证个团队和 Skype for Business 的设备，可以减少遇到设备本身 （这是更可能，例如，带内置便携式计算机扬声器和麦克风） 由于负体验的可能性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1263">By supplying users with devices certified for Teams and Skype for Business, you reduce the likelihood of encountering negative experiences due to the device itself (which is more likely, for example, with built-in laptop speakers and microphones).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1264">有关详细信息，请参阅[认证计划](/SkypeForBusiness/certification/overview)和[合作伙伴解决方案目录](https://partnersolutions.skypeforbusiness.com/solutionscatalog/personal-peripherals-pcs)上的以下文章。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1264">For more information, see these articles on the [certification program](/SkypeForBusiness/certification/overview) and the [partner solutions catalog](https://partnersolutions.skypeforbusiness.com/solutionscatalog/personal-peripherals-pcs).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1265">设备报告用来评估设备用法通过批量和 MOS 得分 （仅限音频），可在客户端 & 设备下的相应模板中找到。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1265">The device reports are used to assess device usage by volume and MOS score (audio only), and can be found in the accompanying templates under Clients & Devices.</span></span> 

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1266">除非您排除联盟参与者数据，这些报表将包括来自联盟的终结点的客户端遥测。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1266">Unless you exclude federated participant data, these reports will include client telemetry from federated endpoints.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1267">若要排除联盟的终结点，您必须添加**第二个租户 ID**设置为贵组织的[租户 ID](#tenant-id)查询筛选器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1267">To exclude federated endpoints, you must add a query filter for **Second Tenant ID** set to your organization’s [tenant ID](#tenant-id).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1268">此外，您可以使用[URL 筛选器](#url-filter)中排除联盟参与者遥测。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1268">ALternatively, you can use a [URL filter](#url-filter) to exclude federated participant telemetry.</span></span>

> [!NOTE] 
> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1269">请务必调整到当前月份月年筛选器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1269">Be sure to adjust the Month Year filter to the current month.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1270">选择**编辑**，然后调整**月年**保存新默认的月份。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1270">Select **Edit**, and adjust **Month Year** to save the new default month.</span></span>

> [!Note]
> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1271">您还可能注意何时查看此报告，您会看到相同的设备报告多次。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1271">You might notice when viewing this report that you see the same device reported multiple times.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1272">这是由于设备报告向 CQD 报告的方式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1272">This is due to the way the device is reported being reported to CQD.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1273">硬件和操作系统区域设置中的差异会导致差异如何报告设备数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1273">Differences in hardware and OS locale cause differences in how device data is reported.</span></span>

##### <a name="diagnostic-alert"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1276">诊断通知</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1276">Diagnostic alert</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1277">如果您收到诊断警报"呼叫下降，导致音频驱动程序"重点关注首先补救这些驱动程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1277">If you received a diagnostic alert “Audio drivers are causing call drops,” focus on remediating those drivers first.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1278">该通知已标识已知的损坏驱动程序均导致调用删除且产生负面影响呼叫可靠性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1278">The alert has identified that known bad drivers are causing calls to drop and are negatively affecting call reliability.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1279">麦克风驱动程序报告 （如上所示），它在客户端 & 设备部分中找到，可用于帮助实现过程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1279">You can use the Microphone-Drivers report (shown above), which is found in the Client & Devices section, to help with the process.</span></span>

##### <a name="remediation"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1280">修正</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1280">Remediation</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1281">通常情况下，您将需要发现和逐步停止使用非认证的设备并将其替换为认证的设备。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1281">Typically, you’ll need to discover and phase out non-certified devices and replace them with certified devices.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1282">检查设备报告时的一些注意事项包括：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1282">Some considerations when reviewing the device reports include:</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1283">使用认证个团队和 for Business 的 Skype 设备？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1283">Are the devices in use certified for Teams and Skype for Business?</span></span> 
-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1284">您可以标识通过[调用分析](https://techcommunity.microsoft.com/t5/Skype-for-Business-Blog/Introducing-Call-Analytics/ba-p/57309)特定设备的用户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1284">You can identify users of a specific device through [Call Analytics](https://techcommunity.microsoft.com/t5/Skype-for-Business-Blog/Introducing-Call-Analytics/ba-p/57309).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1285">检查以确保它们具有最新的设备驱动程序和其设备没有连接通过 USB 集线器或扩展坞分开。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1285">Check to make sure they have the latest device drivers and that their device isn’t connected through a USB hub or docking station.</span></span> 
-   <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1286">使用有多少不同版本的各种驱动程序？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1286">How many different versions of various drivers are in use?</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1287">他们修补定期？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1287">Are they being patched regularly?</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1288">确保的音频、 视频和 Wi-fi 驱动程序修补定期将帮助消除这些作为质量问题的一个来源，并使用户体验更可预测和一致。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1288">Ensuring that audio, video, and Wi-Fi drivers are being patched regularly will help eliminate these as a source of quality issues and make the user experience more predictable and consistent.</span></span>

##### <a name="audio"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1289">音频</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1289">Audio</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1290">下一个任务是确定[认证音频设备](https://partnersolutions.skypeforbusiness.com/solutionscatalog/personal-peripherals-pcs)的总体使用情况。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1290">The next task is to determine the overall usage of [certified audio devices](https://partnersolutions.skypeforbusiness.com/solutionscatalog/personal-peripherals-pcs).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1291">建议至少 80%的所有音频流使用认证音频设备。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1291">We recommend that at least 80 percent of all audio streams use a certified audio device.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1292">最好通过将麦克风设备报告导出到 Excel 计算认证或已批准的设备的使用情况。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1292">This is best accomplished by exporting the microphone devices report to Excel to calculate the usage of certified or approved devices.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1293">组织通常保留所有批准的设备的列表，以便进行筛选和排序数据应变得非常简单。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1293">Organizations typically keep a list of all approved devices, so filtering and sorting the data should be straightforward.</span></span>

##### <a name="video"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1294">视频</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1294">Video</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1295">视频驱动程序很重要，以及保留更新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1295">Video drivers are important to keep updated as well.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1296">确保定期修补视频卡将帮助您排除视频驱动程序作为视频流的质量不佳的一个来源。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1296">Ensuring that video cards are being regularly patched will help exclude video drivers as a source of poor quality for video streams.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1297">使用[认证视频设备](https://partnersolutions.skypeforbusiness.com/solutionscatalog/personal-peripherals-pcs)，有助于确保顺利、 高品质用户体验。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1297">Using [certified video devices](https://partnersolutions.skypeforbusiness.com/solutionscatalog/personal-peripherals-pcs) will help ensure a smooth and high-quality user experience.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1298">被首选支持本机 H.264 编码的视频设备，以减少 CPU 使用率期间视频会议。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1298">Video devices that support H.264 native encoding are preferred, to reduce CPU usage during video conferencing.</span></span>

##### <a name="wi-fi"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1299">Wi-Fi</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1299">Wi-Fi</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1300">Wi-fi 驱动程序还需要在正则节奏以及修补和应包含在您的修补程序的管理策略。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1300">Wi-Fi drivers also need to be patched on a regular cadence as well and should be included in your patch management strategy.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1301">可以通过保持最新 Wi-fi 驱动程序纠正许多质量问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1301">Many quality issues can be corrected by maintaining up-to-date Wi-Fi drivers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1302">有关优化 Wi-fi 基础结构的详细信息，请参阅[关于 Wi-fi 规划这篇文章](/skypeforbusiness/certification/networking-wifi)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1302">For more information about optimizing your Wi-Fi infrastructure, see [this article about Wi-Fi planning](/skypeforbusiness/certification/networking-wifi).</span></span>

## <a name="appendix"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1303">附录</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1303">Appendix</span></span> 

### <a name="office-365-network-connectivity-principles"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1304">Office 365 网络连接原则</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1304">Office 365 network connectivity principles</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1305">规划 Office 365 网络连接网络之前，务必了解用于安全地管理 Office 365 流量和获取最佳性能的连接原则。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1305">Before you begin planning your network for Office 365 network connectivity, it’s important to understand the connectivity principles for securely managing Office 365 traffic and getting the best possible performance.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1306">下面的文章将帮助您了解有关安全地优化 Office 365 网络连接的最新指南：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1306">The following article will help you understand the most recent guidance for securely optimizing Office 365 network connectivity:</span></span>

[<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1307">Office 365 网络连接原则</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1307">Office 365 Network Connectivity Principles</span></span>](https://aka.ms/pnc)

### <a name="planning-for-wi-fi"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1308">规划 Wi-fi</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1308">Planning for Wi-Fi</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1309">Microsoft 的驱动器质量和灵活性到无线网络方法分为三个部分： 端到端规划、 部署和主动维护和操作最佳实践。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1309">Microsoft’s approach to drive quality and agility into the wireless networks comes in three parts: end to end planning, best practices in deployment, and proactive maintenance and operations.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1310">此解决方案简要引导您完成此过程，以确保商业体验企业级的无线 Skype:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1310">This solution brief walks you through this process to ensure an enterprise-class wireless Skype for Business experience:</span></span>

[<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1311">确保业务体验的企业类无线 Skype</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1311">Ensuring an Enterprise Class Wireless Skype for Business Experience</span></span>](https://www.microsoft.com/download/details.aspx?id=47257)

### <a name="lync-networking-guide"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1312">Lync 网络指南</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1312">Lync Networking Guide</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1313">有关更多背景的团队和 Skype 业务网络概念和基本原理对质量的重要性， [Lync Server 2013 网络指南](https://blogs.technet.microsoft.com/nexthop/2013/06/03/lync-server-2013-networking-guide-network-planning-monitoring-and-troubleshooting-with-microsoft-lync-server/)是仍然适用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1313">For more background on the Teams and Skype for Business networking concepts and rationale behind their importance to quality, the [Lync Server 2013 Networking Guide](https://blogs.technet.microsoft.com/nexthop/2013/06/03/lync-server-2013-networking-guide-network-planning-monitoring-and-troubleshooting-with-microsoft-lync-server/) is still applicable.</span></span>

### <a name="network-performance-requirements"></a><span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1314">网络性能要求</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1314">Network performance requirements</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1315">Ip 电话 （音频、 视频和应用程序共享） 实时媒体质量会显著影响的端到端网络连接质量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1315">The quality of real-time media (audio, video, and application sharing) over IP is greatly affected by the quality of end-to-end network connectivity.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1316">对于最佳工作组或业务媒体质量的 Skype，您的网络必须满足以下网络性能指标。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1316">For optimal Teams or Skype for Business media quality, your network must meet the following network performance metrics.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1317">_表 12-网络性能要求_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1317">_Table 12 - Network performance requirements_</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1318">指标</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1318">Metric</span></span>                            | <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1319">客户端到 Microsoft 边缘</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1319">Client to Microsoft Edge</span></span>           | <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1320">客户边缘到 Microsoft 边缘</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1320">Customer Edge to Microsoft Edge</span></span>    |
|-----------------------------------|------------------------------------|------------------------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1321">延迟 （一种方法）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1321">Latency (one way)</span></span>                 | <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1322">\<50 ms</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1322">\<50 ms</span></span>                            | <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1323">\<30 ms</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1323">\<30 ms</span></span>                            |
| <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1324">延迟 （RTT 或往返时间）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1324">Latency (RTT, or round-trip time)</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1325">\<100 毫秒</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1325">\<100 ms</span></span>                           | <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1326">\<60 毫秒</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1326">\<60 ms</span></span>                            |
| <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1327">突发数据包丢失</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1327">Burst packet loss</span></span>                 | <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1328">\<任何 200 毫秒间隔期间的 10%</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1328">\<10% during any 200-ms interval</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1329">\<任何 200 毫秒间隔期间 1%</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1329">\<1% during any 200-ms interval</span></span>    |
| <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1330">数据包丢失</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1330">Packet loss</span></span>                       | <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1331">\<任何 15 秒间隔期间 1%</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1331">\<1% during any 15-sec interval</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1332">\<0.1 任何 15 秒间隔期间 %</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1332">\<0.1% during any 15-sec interval</span></span>  |
| <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1333">数据包间到达抖动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1333">Packet inter-arrival Jitter</span></span>       | <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1334">\<任何 15 秒间隔期间 30 ms</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1334">\<30 ms during any 15-sec interval</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1335">\<在任何 15 秒时间间隔 15 ms</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1335">\<15 ms during any 15-sec interval</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1336">数据包重新排序</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1336">Packet reorder</span></span>                    | <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1337">\<0.05%无序的数据包</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1337">\<0.05% out-of-order packets</span></span>       | <span data-ttu-id="d5b37-1338">\<0.01%无序的数据包</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b37-1338">\< 0.01% out-of-order packets</span></span>      |
